Early Work · January 2018

First Love

Prose · BTS university AU — Part 1 of 2

First Love.
𝒿𝓊𝓈𝓉 𝒷𝑒𝒸𝒶𝓊𝓈𝑒 𝓉𝒽𝑒𝓎 𝓌𝑒𝓇𝑒 𝓂𝑒𝒶𝓃𝓉 𝓉𝑜 𝒷𝑒 𝒹𝑜𝑒𝓈𝓃'𝓉 𝓂𝑒𝒶𝓃 𝓉𝒽𝑒𝓎'𝓇𝑒 𝓂𝑒𝒶𝓃𝓉 𝓉𝑜 𝓈𝓉𝒶𝓎.

in which two people fall in love through passion, only for their passion to be the same thing that tore them apart.

First Love was wrote from January 25, 2018 to August 10, 2018.
The rewriting process began on May 26, 2019.

4476752943225

하나; the corner of my memory
An exhausted yawn leaves her lips, her head dipping down to nearly fall onto the desk she sat at. The ticklish feeling of her hair gently grazing the sides of her face, having had fell out of the messy bun, causes her to startle back into reality. Raising her hands to rub her tired eyes, trying to fully regain her conscience, she tried to push the fact her body was desperately begging for rest away. Despite the thought she liked to think she never got tired, deeming herself nocturnal, she couldn’t help but be fatigued from the never ending day she’d had.
However, unlike her body that was pleading for sleep, she didn’t have the willpower to grant it such, not yet. Eyes directing back to the opened journal before her, she knew the work she insisted that must be done couldn’t wait. Such a type of work that was deeply important to her, not because of university, but because it was her passion.
Rising from her desk, her feet pad across the plush of the dorms carpet, her journal and pen clenched tightly in her hands. With her brain working at an irregularly quick speed, many thoughts tended to wander in her mind at such times. Her back hits the soft of the mattress as she falls onto it, trying to regain her thoughts and forget about her weariness as she diverts her attention back to the paper on her lap, focus on the song draft.
Loving music with an intensity as large as hers, many would presume that when she went to university, it was exactly what she’d be majoring in. Although this would’ve been the original plan, to her dismay, her parents hadn’t sought her ideals to be realistic - as they put it. In the end, she’d went with her second option, being journalism. It was her second hobby, after all.
Even then, she tended to be caught up with most of her classes. So, in her free time, she liked to write music, that she didn't show to anyone except for a special someone. A certain someone that she trusted more than anything.
Setting her chin in the palm of her hand, eyebrows creasing downward as she contemplates harshly. Of course, song-writing was something that took immense concentration and serious scrutiny. But for her, it always seemed to come naturally, like the words just flowed through her veins, like they were a part of her and she was only transforming them onto the paper. To her dismay, however, on that particular day it was as if they’d dried out, like someone had drained her of her usual lyrical talent. This was becoming rather frustrating, as she huffs in vexation, repeatedly hitting her pen on the page and closing her eyes to fully drench in her own thoughts.
Rapid blinking of a light seemed to go off in her brain, the excitement sending a vigorous signal through her body like a spark. Sitting up straight, she was so excited she nearly fell of the bed she was upon. Gripping the pen so hard it was bound to break under her tight hold, her eyes narrow in engrossment as she scribbles down the words that had come to her like her life depended on it.
Knock knock knock
The abrupt sound echoed through the practically empty dorm, her hand halting it’s previous angrily writing motion. Blinking a few times as she processes who could possibly be at her door, she shook her head, deciding that whoever it was - she wasn’t currently invested in either way. With that in mind, she went back to the intense writing session she was having. Biting down on her bottom lip, she carefully thought about how to word the hook of the song.
Only when a second later, another few knocks were heard. Before she could even begin to decide if she wanted to ignore those as well, the person knocked again, and again. Eventually, she felt as if her brain was going to burst as she heaved out an displeased sigh, already having an idea of just who was at her front door as such an ungodly hour.
Annoyed that her absorption in her writing was destroyed, she knew that he wasn’t going away anytime soon. With no other choice, she hurriedly makes a last note on the page in her journal, just as another couple knocks broke through her brain. Groaning impatiently, she spins on her heel to walk across the small room.
Completely unimpressed, her tiresome expression didn’t fade as she was faced with the exact human she expected to be standing on the other side of the door. The devious smile on his face was enough to give her an idea of what he was there for, and she’d never dreaded anything more.
"Taehyung," she whines, turning away to walk back further into her dorm, her tone almost pleading with him, "I don't want to go out."
At first, such a lively smile had obliterated, presumably from her denial of his request that had yet to even be asked. With eyes peering into hers, the brown glistening from the light, his face went from complete disappointment - to looking aggrieved instead.
"It's the third week of the month, remember? The party tonight is at that gross sorority," he informs her in a knowing tone, as if he was bewildered and despondent that she didn’t already know this. After a second, his words sunk in, the realization washing over the petite girl’s face before him in waves. No doubt, with how drowsy she was, she indeed hadn’t remembered something like that.
"Oh, right,” she hums in understanding, brushing hair out of her face as she thinks a bit before something else had come to mind. Why exactly was he here if it wasn’t to drag her to some ridiculous sorority party? Eyes full of confusion, they find a way back to the jumpy boy before her, mumbling out the question in scepticism, “so what exactly are you here for then?”
With that huge box smile appearing on his lips again in no time, he’d walked further into her dorm much like she had moments ago, dramatically pushing past her since she’d been in the walkway. Not a word left his lips even as he did so, and as she slightly stumbles to the side from the impact, she scoffs, glaring at him for the fact he just did that (even though he’d done it a million times before with how big of a drama queen he tended to be.) Taehyung had only casually hummed to himself a song she didn’t recognize as he grabs her back pack that was beside her bed.
"Tae," she snaps as he began to shove her things in it, still not saying anything about what his intentions were and why. 
Hand just over her journal that she’d been writing in only minutes ago, his brown eyes widen with curiosity. The sight of him reaching out to grab it caused her own to nearly fall out of their sockets, knowing she would never hear the end of it if he read her current work. Just when his hand was over the opened journal, she lunged forward to snatch it away from his clutching eyes. Closing the object and holding it safely in her possession, Taehyung seemed to snap out of his packing frenzy from the sudden action as his soft irises find their way back to her stern expression.
Blinking at her a few times, it seemed to take him a moment to even remember what she asked in the first place. When he does, his mouth forms an o shape, and he knits his brows together as he informs, "we're having a sleepover." There was a sense of puzzlement in his tone, as he’d figured she would already be able to gather that. After all, it wasn’t uncommon for their entire friend group to get together, no matter the time. Most of them already living together, there were only two of them who didn’t, with her being one of them. It was why when they were having one of those nights, it was his job to come get her whether she was asleep or doing anything else - because every third Friday night of every month was that night. When there was no college party to attend - or at least not one they wanted to - they’d all just go hang out instead.
A sigh leaves her lips as she looks down at her journal, thinking about how much she'd wanted to finish the song. Some time with all of her friends was definitely well needed, though, she realized as she looked to Taehyung again to confirm, but he'd already went back to packing.
She sighs as he already knew she would be going whether she wanted to or not. Once he finished packing everything he knew of her needing, he zipped up her bag, that childish box smile finding a way to his lips once again as he holds it out to her.
Rolling her eyes at his kid-like attitude, she took her bag from his hand, shoving her journal and pen in the front pocket. She was still going to finish the song despite of her previous thoughts, as she realized that certain someone could definitely help her with that. The sudden remembrance was enough to disintegrate her bummed behavior, replaced with the eagerness of seeing him.
“Let’s go then!” she cheerily hums, already heading out the door and into the hall of the college dorm building. Taehyung’s now astonished eyes follow her, but she paid no attention to the boggled expression on his face from her abrupt change in attitude.
Shrugging to himself, he followed her out into the hall just as jumpily. Jingling his car keys in his hand, he watches as one of his best friend’s frantically locked the door to her dorm. Before he could open his mouth to ask her the lingering question on his mind while they walked to the elevator, she hadn’t given him a chance to when she broke into a run straight for it.
Gawking at the sight of her running for once, he jogged a bit to meet with her at the large elevator doors. With the way she would twirl her hair around her finger while waiting for the doors to open before them, her green eyes gleaming up at the ceiling as if she was day-dreaming - he had a perfect idea as to what she was so riled up about - or more like who.
It was why that mischievous smirk spreads over his lips as he looks down to her, his eyes already shining with a teasing glint once they step in the elevator. Having had been involved in pushing the right floor button, the girl hadn’t looked to him until he’d spoke the words, “someone’s suddenly excited.”
Resisting the urge to knee him in the balls was rather difficult, as when she finally looked to him after he dared to say such, only for Taehyung to send a suggestive wink her way. Glaring at him, clearly unimpressed, Katarina crosses her arms over her chest, looking away to the closed elevator doors as she scoffs, “Oh, don’t even start with me.”
Although he knew why she was saying this, he still found himself giggling out from her sassy tone of voice, asking in fake misunderstanding, “what, why?”
But it was obvious he already knew, and she knew he did without even seeing the hysterical look on his face. Shaking her head, she rolls her eyes, playfully hitting his arm as they stand in the moving elevator, “you get a boner every time you see Eden, and you’re trying to tease me about me and Yoongi’s relationship?”
Trying to keep her cool demeanor, it was becoming rather hard since whenever anyone tended to do something as mere as mentioning her and Yoongi being in something like a relationship, it played with her heart in undeniable ways. One of those times was then, as she hurriedly turned away from her friend to hide the tint that was spreading to her cheeks. They didn’t even have a relationship, really.
Much to her dismay, Taehyung was already aware of how red her cheeks were just because of how well he knew her. In between snickers leaving his lips at her facial expression and her adolescent words, he deemed this out as if he was some sort of genius, “yeah, but at least I don’t deny that I get one, unlike a certain someone.”
Never did he stop making idiotic jokes, and even though she knew this, she still found herself turning to look at him again in disbelief. It wasn’t that he was stupid, it was more of an act, but she still wanted to face palm at his intellectual level, “what are you even suggesting?” she’s mumbling in bewilderment, “that I get a hard on everytime I see Yoongi?!”
From this, he’d burst into uncontrollable laughter, the air seeming to be drained from his lungs as he had to bend over, holding his stomach in pain from the hysterical sounds that wouldn’t stop leaving his lips. Trying to contain herself, Katarina sighs, “you know, Taehyung, I’d hate to inform you, but I don’t have a penis.”
He’d paused his laughing fit to look at her, and at the sight of the humored look on his face, she felt herself giggling too. The both of them would probably look like psycho’s to anyone else, which was why they had to rush to calm themselves when the elevator had dinged, and the doors opened before them.
Wiping fake tears from under his eyes, Taehyung is still regaining himself as they make their way out of the elevator. Feeling like he was breathing normally once again, he finally voiced out as they’re padding across the lobby, “No, I mean that any time I bring up you two having a thing, you get all defensive.”
She hadn’t gotten a chance to reply since they were leaving the building. The cold air shoots goosebumps up her pale skin, traveling up her spine in shivers, as her green eyes wander to the night sky. There was a comfortable silence, other than the jingling sound of Tae’s keys, and the stars seemed to twinkle down at her, creating a euphoric symphony whilst they make their way to the car. Trying to gather her thoughts, Taehyung kept glancing at her every second, awaiting her reply.
Just when they were reaching his car, only then had she finally regained her thoughts to admit dimly, “I don’t even know if we have a thing.” She hadn’t noticed her friend’s apologetic gaze as she then walks to the passenger side, swinging open the door and climbing in the Toyota, her hands rubbing her forearms as an attempt to warm herself from the cold outside weather.
Climbing in the driver’s seat, shoving the keys in the ignition of the vehicle, Taehyung had heaved out a sigh as the car engine revs to life. There was another ping of quiet between them, when he finally looks to her again as he backs out of the parking lot, stating, “you know, Yoongi-hyung really likes you, right?”

Leaning her head against the window, the glass was freezing cold from the outside weather, sending a shiver through her body. However, due to the disorganized thoughts in her mind that she was desperately trying to sort through.

"I guess so," she only shrugs in reply after a few minutes, before deciding to change the subject as she was dreading the current one, "so why do you seem extra jumpy, anyways?” now she was the one with the teasing tone as she reaches out to poke his arm, “Does it have to do with my certain best friend?" She hummed, raising a brow as she referred to Eden.
She could say very sincerely that she loved Taehyung's and Eden’s relationship. They'd become instant friends, and Eden never shut up about him – just to find out he never shut up about her either. They were the type of couple that made up for each other's flaws in a perfect way, which was something she longed for.
Well, they weren't a couple – yet. 
Even though they might as well be, they had yet to make it official. But that didn’t mean she wasn’t about to still refer to them as such.
Taehyung is silent as he drove, causing her to look to him in confusion. He was never this quiet, as usually he never had to think before speaking, he just spoke his mind whenever he felt like it. Which was why this was weird to her.
As she stared at his expression, she noticed he seemed to actually be in deep thought about something. He looked rather stressed, and troubled, which was something you never saw in someone as carefree as Kim Taehyung. 
Unable to see the way he’d bite down on his bottom lip every few seconds in clear perturbance, she was too curious of what was on his mind so suddenly, "Tae," She spoke his name as a question to get his attention, and his brown anxious eyes find a way to hers, "are you alright?"

Snapping out of his daze, he turns onto the street the guys lived on. They all lived together as roommates, except for Eden and her. The guys begged them to come be roommates with them, but they both decided to just stay back at the university, knowing they probably wouldn't even attend class half the time if they all lived together.

"Oh, yeah," he shakes his head, "the guys and I just have something important to tell you and Eden."

She only grew more confused as this information, "but you were so excited about it like, five minutes ago?" How could his mood drastically deter out of nowhere? It wasn’t something she ever saw out of him, and it was having her feeling rather blank as she stared up at his side profile since he was still focusing on driving.

Taehyung rolls his eyes as his hands clutch the steering wheel a little tighter, before he confidently states, "no, I was excited because I got to see you, and," that smile spread over his lips again and his chocolate eyes brightened as he then dreamily concluded, "not to mention, I'm another minute closer to seeing Eden again."

Katarina wrinkled her nose at his last comment in fake disgust, but she couldn't deny how adorable his liking towards her really was. Before she could say anything more to his suspicious behavior moments ago, he was parking in front of the house the boys lived in.

Hurriedly climbing out of the car since Taehyung was awaiting to lock the vehicle, she’d grabbed her bag that contained her phone and other essentials. The cold air tickled her as she rushed through it to where he was now making his way up the sidewalk to the two-story house the seven boys resided in. Hiking her bag further up her shoulder, Katarina takes her spot next to Taehyung on the front porch, listening to the beep of the car indicating it was now locked, followed by him vigorously knocking on the door since he never brought his keys.

As she stands behind him waiting for it to be opened, you can hear the commotion from inside the house. Not even to mention the loud music being played, her friends were definitely abruptive people - only god knew how they didn’t get noise complaints from any neighbors.

"They’re here!" yells are heard before the sound of heavy, quick footsteps, and the front door is soon opened to reveal the majority of her best friends, all standing there with bright expressions written on their faces.

Her best friend is the first one to jump forward eagerly to hug her, having had pushed past the others violently. Calling out her name in excitement, Katarina had only giggled as she accepts the embrace, feeling a lot better now that she was in the presence of her favorite people.

"We all know who you really want to hug," she coaxes, winking playfully as she pulls away from the hug, motioning to Taehyung who was standing there beside her. Eden’s eyes were confused before she looked to the boy, who's cheeks flushed under her gaze.

"Look at him, he’s blushing!" The exclaim of Hoseok was heard as some of the boys began laughing at their whipped friend, all gathered around in the entryway.

Jin made a fake sobbing sound as they closed the door after the two had piled inside, looking to Tae and Eden who dramatically ran into each other's embrace to spite the other's amusement, "my child is growing up," He gushed sympathetically on behalf of one of the biggest inside jokes in the group.

A chorus of chuckles is spread over the friend group from their eldest’s jokes, unable to contain themselves whenever it was spoken about. Katarina had been the only one not giggling, not paying much attention as her green eyes scan across all of the friends. In the midst of hugging them all and greeting them, she’d realized matter of factly that someone was missing - someone who happened to be rather important to her.

Namjoon’s the one who firstly notices her dull expression at the realization of this, and raises a brow in wonder as they're all taking their seats in the living room to watch a movie. Everyone basically had their own spot at this point. Namjoon and Jin sat together on the floor, Eden and Tae took one of the sofas on the side, Jimin, Jungkook, and Hoseok took the large couch in the middle, and Yoongi and Katarina always sat on the sofa on the opposite side. Every spot in the room was filled, as Jimin and Taehyung began to talk about what movie they wanted to watch tonight – every spot that wasn’t Yoongi’s.

Shifting drearily in her lone seat on the sofa, Katarina purses her lips in contemplation. No doubt, she probably looked rather sad there as she could feel Namjoon’s empathetic gaze on her every once in a while in the midst of everyone else talking about the choice of film they wanted.

"Yoongi-hyung, your girlfriend’s here!" he suddenly yells at the best of his ability, causing everyone to either start snickering from what he’d called her or give him a weird look.

Not having the energy to deal with her insistent friends, she didn’t bother to correct what he’d referred to her as to Yoongi. Instead, she sat and waited for him to show up from the place she knew he was in – but if that was where he was, she realized, there was no way he even heard him in the first place.
"I can keep you company!" Jungkook is calling from beside Hoseok and Jimin, having had noticed she was by herself because of Yoongi’s absence thanks to Namjoon’s words. He's about to get up when Jimin doesn't let him, laying his head across his lap so he couldn’t move. The youngest’s eyes widen at his friend’s action, looking down to him in misunderstanding, a pout evident on his lips.

Jimin mouths something that Katarina couldn't make out to Jungkook, who only nods reluctantly in response, but didn’t look too pleased with whatever he’d been told.

She sighs, rising to her own feet. Everyone probably already knew where she was heading, but she decided to only mumble as she left anyways, "I'm going to find him," not wanting to speak too loud since the movie they were watching was starting.

The last thing her eyes were met with before she’d entered the long hall was the sight of the proximity between Namjoon and Jin practically being nonexistent. It was a sweet vision, causing a small smile to take over her face as she shakes her head in disbelief. Everyone swore behind the two’s backs that they clearly had a thing for each other, hence the commonly used ‘family’ joke in the group. But they always denied it whenever you brought it up to them, acting as if it was the most appalling thing they’d ever heard.
Meanwhile, Taehyung and Eden were nonchalantly cuddling on the wooden floor atop a heap of what looked like a billion blankets, along with one drenched over them. His arm was wrapped securely around her as if he was afraid to let go, like she’d disappear into the wind if he dared to do such. The undeniably adorable way those two were with each other warmed her heart as she gushes at them, nothing could make her feel more joyous than seeing her best friend so content with someone. It was a match made in heaven.

Shaking her thoughts away, she leaves the room; but not before grabbing the most important thing, descending the hall towards where he was.

Humming a melody to herself, it wasn’t long that her feet had padded down the carpeted hall until her eyes were met with the familiar door. A light titter leaves her lips as she read that same sign that hung on the door with cheap tape, printed out on a simple white sheet with the generic Microsoft Word lettering.
Min Yoongi Genius Lab

She chuckles at the name like every other time she saw it. He was just so – lame to her, in a completely irresistible way she couldn't seem to explain without writing an essay.

Putting her ear to the door, although she should’ve already known it was impossible to hear through the sound proofed room, she’d tried anyway. Her insides were burning with wonder, wishing she could hear whatever he must be doing in the studio she stood outside of.
Taking a step back, Katarina purses her lips as she has a serious debate with herself. He wouldn’t mind her coming in at all, and although she knew the passcode and could easily type it in and enter herself, she still had her doubts. The last thing she ever wanted to do was invade someone as introverted as Yoongi’s privacy, even though it was impossible for her to do so - but she was too naive to comprehend such a thing.

Like her, he loved music with a strong passion. The two of them were similar in more ways than one, which was part of the reason their friends forced them together so much. It was why you’d find him spending sleepless nights in his cozy studio that he’d had built specifically for his hobby, songwriting and making songs all by himself. That is, when she wasn’t there to cut in.

Finally managing to gather the courage as if she hadn’t already done this a thousand times before, she exhales deeply, raising her fist to clash it against the door a few times. When she knocks loudly enough so he’d hear, her hands fall back to her side, and she awkwardly stood there, her eyes nervously wandering everywhere that wasn’t where he was bound to appear within seconds.
However, when there’s no reply, the guileless girl realized he probably had his headphones in. Shaking her head out of disappointment that she didn’t think of it earlier, she raised a finger to push the small button that was located beside the keypad, which alerted him through his headset that someone was outside the door.

Feeling the tingling nerves shooting through her veins like fireworks, she shifts from one foot to the other as she awaits an answer. She should’ve known nothing could ever prepare her for the presence of someone so glorious in her eyes, and that was only proven further when the large door was swung open before her.

It always took her a moment to take in the sight of Min Yoongi, and she was sure it always would. His hair was messy, and a beanie was lazily placed over his head. You could tell he was tired, but like her, refused to sleep due to being a night owl.

There was a sour look on his face, presumably from the assumption he’d made that the other person standing on the opposite side of the door would not be her, but one of the guys endlessly annoying him like they did constantly. It takes a moment for the rotten expression to fade, turning into one of shock once his eyes burn into her delicate gaze.
As if an aura of innocence had washed over him, Yoongi’s eyes soften that of a kitten. There was a silence that fell, and she was waiting for him to invite her in or say anything in the first place. But when he doesn’t within the first few seconds, the brunette had found herself feeling rather sensitive under his messianic stare. It was like he was taking in every detail of her features, as if he didn’t see her practically a billion times a week already. Although she was flattered, and embarrassed, it was out of the ordinary for him.
When he was still gaping at her with those eyes of his, her heart was beginning to shut down. Deeming she was unable to take it anymore, she cleared her throat loudly, and Yoongi seemed to be slapped out of his alternate reality.
Coughing a bit from the tension in the air, he slides across the floor to the side, motioning with his hand for her to come inside. Offering him a thankful, small smile, she enters the familiar studio, hearing the click of him closing the door behind her before he explains casually as if he wasn’t just immensely staring into her soul, “Oh, I didn’t know you were here already.”
Even though a part of her was wondrous, the last thing she was going to do was ask about it. Instead, she falls into one of the rolly chairs he had next to his own, her eyes raking over the decorations that hung on the walls that she knew all too well. After a short thought, she intimates, “it’s alright,” her heartbeat had increased at the sound of a chair sinking, knowing he’d just sat in his own next to her. The scent of that same cologne he always wore trailed into her nostrils as she then observes, eyes scanning over the many papers he had scattered across his desk, “you seem busy.”

When there isn’t a reply for a noticeable amount of time, her curious green irises divert to the boy sitting beside her. It wasn’t uncommon for Yoongi to not be very vocal, in fact he was just a rather quiet soul, but as she peered up at his side profile, it was obvious there was something out of the normal going on. She could tell from how well she knew him, with the way he seemed to be staring into nothingness in deep contemplation, pursing his lips every once in a while, and puffing out his cheeks before he would deeply exhale. It reminded her of the weird act Taehyung had put on earlier during the drive to the house, there was definitely something fishy happening. But she was completely clueless as to what it could be, as she thought hard on it herself, thinking back.
Only then was her mind reminded of the apparent thing the boys all had to inform her and Eden of. That must have something to do with it, she’d concluded mentally. Her confidence coming out of nowhere, she was about to speak up and ask him about it herself, when he beat her to the speaking process.

“Yeah,” he finally responds nonchalantly, “I’m working on something special.”
It was unattainable how many times she had heard Yoongi inform her that he was working on a song, but never had she heard that it was specifically for someone - and someone special, at that. Hearing such an explanation so casually had her thrown into vast misunderstanding as her brows knitted together.
Opening her mouth to ask who that person might be, possibly out of jealousy, he’d turned to her, posing a question before a word could leave her own lips, “What about you, what’ve you been working on?”

Her eyes trail away from his to the journal that lied in her lap. Mind wandering back to the song she had been working so hard on recently, Katarina worriedly asked herself if she really liked it enough to show him.

Unable to make up her mind, she replied unconfidently, tone doubtless, "Oh, something I've been working on for the past few days, although now that I think about it I'm not sure—" she's cut off when he gently slips the journal out of her small hands.

Her nerves only grow as she doesn't object, knowing he would read it anyways. She only watches as he flips through the pages to her most recent song.

His expression was focused as his eyes skimmed over the words, quickly at first before he'd slow down and read some lyrics over again. Yoongi's face was unreadable to her, and the worry that the song was probably silly caused her to look down to her feet.

Oh god, why did I let this happen? She closed her eyes as they sat in silence, waiting for him to finish. The song suddenly felt so cringe-worthy to her now that it was in his hands. Not to mention what it was about, there was no telling what he was thinking.

As her eyes slowly opened, she dared to look to the boy that sat in front of her. She hoped he wouldn't be paying attention to her when she did so, but sure enough his chocolate eyes were focused right on her. Their eyes meet and she felt nervous under his gaze. The ways Min Yoongi made her feel were unexplainable.

She's about to go right out and tell him how she knew the first part of the song (also the only part she had so far,) was absolutely horrible. But before she can, that big gummy smile takes over his lips, and his next words surprise her, "I like it."

"R—really?" she was rather astonished, eyes wide in disbelief.

He only nods curtly in reply, still holding the journal in his hands. Instead of giving it back, he's suddenly turning to face his desk. This seemed to surprise her even more, worried about what he was doing and if he was going to insult something written. But she couldn't lie that she was also excited at the thought he might be helping her write it, or even adding something.

Before she could even ask which one it was that he was doing, he was picking up the pen she had attached to the journal. Clicking it, he's re-reading the verse again, "Is this the first verse?"

She nervously gazed at her pen in his hand that was hovering above the words she'd worked so hard on the last few nights. "Uh, yeah," she finally managed to reply.

He didn't even glance at her from how focused he was. All she knew to do was watch him in admiration. His love for music was inspiring to her, and no doubt everyone else in the friend group.

The sound of him scribbling out some words, and replacing others, was heard as he mumbles, "I think it would sound better if you removed this – and then put – this," he kept pausing between each pen stroke. Katarina honestly had no idea what he was even crossing out, she just trusted him that much.

Plus, she was glad he wasn't asking her why she wrote it in the first place.

Finishing what he wanted to fix, Yoongi clicks the pen again, setting it down on the journal. He spoke rather proudly, "There, I improved it a bit, not that it needed much. I really like it." He attached the pen back to the journal, handing it to her.

She felt relieved as she set it back on her lap. Sending him a half-hearted smile, "Thank you, that means a lot."

He'd been looking at something on one of his computer screens when she'd spoke. There was a moment of silence except for the sound of him clicking furiously.

Soon, he turned back to her in his fancy wheelie-chair. As she met his eyes, figuring the conversation about her song was over, he looked rather serious. This scared her a bit as she shifted uncomfortably under his gaze. Why is he looking at me like that?!

"Katarina," her name left his lips, and the way it came off his tongue made her want to hear it a thousand times more. When he posed a sudden question she was hoping wouldn't have to hear, "If it's okay for me to ask, who's the song about?"

Her gaze instantly goes to the ground, trying to hide her bulging eyes of horror. To think she'd almost got away without him asking a stupid question like that. What did she say here? Should she tell him the truth?

The words she heard from her friends basically every day filled her thoughts. Was it true someone as flawless as Min Yoongi could genuinely have a thing for her, or did they just always tell her that because they knew how much she liked him? The question frustrated her as she tried to think of what to say.

She was a nervous mess unable to find words when she realized how quiet she'd been for a long time. Yoongi was looking at her expectantly when she met his gaze again.

"Uh – no one," she blurts, before scolding herself mentally. Are you stupid? It's obviously about someone. "I can't tell you."

His forehead wrinkled as his brows furrowed, clearly confused at her reaction. "Oh, alright," he had a different tone in his voice when he spoke next. She couldn't tell what it was – disappointment? Relief?

She felt incredibly awkward now. They both sit there for a few minutes, and she purses her lips as she tried to think of anything to possibly say.

Ding.

The sound of her phone going of almost made her jump in excitement due to the fact it was something to get her out of the situation she was in. Shifting to pull it out of her pocket, she read the text from her friend.

Mama Jin: u & yoongi come back. the guys & I have smthn important to tell u & hails.

Mama Jin: also tae & hailey have been making out and being all lovey for the past thirty minutes

She found herself chuckling at the last text.

Mama Jin: do u know how much of a pain it is holding ur hand over whiney jungkooks eyes for this long

Pushing her nerves away as she wasn't focused on her song anymore but instead this 'important thing' they had to tell her and Hailey, she met his gaze with slight ease, "Jin texted, it's time to tell Hails and I this 'big announcement'," she made quotations with her fingers.

At the mention of it, the tired boy tensed up. He did this when something bothered or worried him, and right then he looked like a rather large mix of both.

She decides to not say anything as they leave the studio, remembering how Tae was being about it, also. What could it possibly be that had them getting so nerve wrecked about it?

Walking into the room, she saw the lamps that were scattered around the room lit up to dimly provide some sight. The movie they'd been watching had no doubt ended, and looking over everyone, the guys all seemed the same way – nervous, tense, afraid. What the hell was up with them?

Hails seemed to notice how they were acting, too. She shifted in Tae's lap to meet her best friend's gaze, giving her the look that meant the exact thing she was thinking. Katarina only knows to reply with a confused shrug.

Her and Yoongi take their seats, and silence fell over the room as the low conversations had stopped. They were all exchanging glances with each other, as if unsure who should say it.

Their nervous faces were scaring both the girls more and more by the second. Katarina couldn't seem to think of what it could be as she glanced to the boy that sat beside her, who was just staring at his feet, biting his lip.

Her mind wanted to scream about how pretty Yoongi looked in that moment, but there were more important things to worry about.

The sound of Namjoon clearing his throat loudly caused their gazes to shift to him. He rose from his feet, beginning to pace around, "So, you guys know how we all love music right?"

He looks to the girls for confirmation, and they slowly nod. Neither of them had any idea where this was going.

"Well, uh, we had this really stupid idea," oh no, "we talked about it a lot, and we – um, want to go to Big Hit Entertainment Studios and uh – audition," he started stuttering and their eyes bulged.

Katarina was lost for words, so Hails said her thoughts for her as she practically yelled, "you what?!" She turned in Tae's lap to fix her eyes on him, as if asking 'what the fuck is he talking about.'

She tried to control her thoughts and take them seriously. It was very real, she had to tell herself as she noticed all their faces.

"You mean like, to be a boy group or something?" She asks, figuring that was probably the answer but just making sure.

A few of them nod in unison, exchanging more looks. They could tell the girls were confused and unconvinced. The guys all like to dance sometimes, and they all sang songs for fun. Not to mention how Yoongi loved music so much he had his own studio. But this, this wasn't what they'd expected.

Hoseok suddenly jumps to his feet, walking to the center of the room and rolling up his sleeves. "We've been practicing building our stamina and being able to sing," he says, before starting to do a dance she recognized from SHINee.

And sure enough, he did pretty well.

Hails stared at Hoseok as he went back to his seat. Slowly, she asked, "So, you guys want to be the next Big Bang, or what?"

Most of them nodded at this vigorously, eyes wide. It was clear this meant a lot to them. The main thing about them all being close friends – was they had to support each other. Especially when it came to their dreams. This meant a lot to them.

"You guys are for real about this?" Hailey is raising a brow as the looks at them all.

"Of course we are," Jimin says with that angelic smile of his.

Jungkook looks to Yoongi, who was still staring at his feet, "That's why Yoongi's been in his studio so much. He's been writing songs for us."

This caused her gaze to shift to the boy that sat beside her, who still didn't look up. She tried to sit and imagine all of her friends on stage, dancing and singing. It sort of fit them, in an alternate-universe sort of way.

When she looks back to everyone, Hailey is staring at her. They have some sort of conversation with their eyes, as if asking if they were to agree with the guys decision or not.

Katarina shrugs to her best friend, before looking back to the guys' hopeful eyes. "I believe in you guys."

At these words leaving her lips, Hailey shifts in Tae's lap, saying confidently, "I do, too. You can all sing rather well," she looks to the boy she's sitting on, "especially Tae."

Her compliment to him caused his grin to appear, and he was leaning in to kiss her nose when Jin's screaming voice was heard. The tall boy flew to his feet to put his hands over Jungkook's eyes. "Seriously, not in front of the child!" He jokes, but you could barely tell from how genuine he sounded.

Jungkook was trying to pry Jin's hands from his eyes but his grip was rather tight, "I'm not a child, hyung!" He complains, clearly upset with all the teasing he constantly had to face about being the maknae.

Hailey was giggling as she pulls away from her love, her eyes on Jin, "Stop acting like your such a good parent, you literally told Hoseok he was a mistake."

Releasing his eyes from Jungkook's face, he was plopping onto the couch again next to Namjoon, "don't talk about it," is all he says. They all start laughing, recalling the time Jin had told Hoseok he was an accident because he was annoying him so badly with the whole 'motherly Jin' joke.

It's silent, when Jimin speaks up to the girls, "so you guys are really okay with it?"

Katarina nods from her stance on the sofa, about to speak when a wave of cold air hit her from the degrees in the room. She swore the guys always had all the fans on full blast despite the fact it was the middle of January.

Rubbing her arms, she finally confirms to them all, "Yeah, you guys are just auditioning. We believe in you, you'll do great." Although as she thought about it, not all of the guys really even sang. Min Yoongi seriously agreed to sing and dance for an audition? It sounded crazy to her.

Suddenly, the room erupts into excited screams and cheers. The guys are all hugging each other and exchanging high fives. This caused the two girls to only smile to themselves at how happy their friends were about this.

Her eyes widen a bit in surprise, and she instantly replies as she looks to him, "Sure!" The studio was probably a couple of hours away, and god knew how awful car rides with the guys were. But she'd never seen a huge, professional studio like that before, it would definitely be an amazing experience. Plus she wanted to cheer her best friends on.

This causes that gummy smile to spread over his lips, "Thank you for supporting us."

She couldn't help but return the smile, melting at how cute he was. "Always, Yoongi."

A loud cat whistle is heard from right in front of them. This causes the two to look up, only for a huge blanket to be thrown over them. The sofa was small enough as it is, but she hadn't seemed to notice how relatively closer they'd gotten.

"Warm up your girlfriend, she's freezing to death, Yoongi," Taehyung is shaking his head disapprovingly.

"Yeah, you don't want her to be like your soul, now do you?" Hoseok added, a playful smile hinting on his lips as the others start laughing at his comment.

Meanwhile, Katarina's cheeks heated up as she slowly let her gaze fall on Yoongi. He wasn't looking at her, but instead was sending a harsh death glare to the culprit of the blanket-thrower.

This was no doubt Taehyung. Under Yoongi's gaze his eyes bulged, and he pointed a finger accusingly, "Look at him – he's gonna hurt me!" Before anyone knew it, he was running out of the room screaming like some sort of child.

They were all laughing, some holding their stomachs in pain as Tae's screams were heard all the way down the hall. Jin was shaking his head, holding a hand to it. His eyes fall on Hailey, "I don't see why you like him."

She shrugs, "Sometimes I'm not sure either," before leaving the room to most likely get her soulmate.

Katarina looked back to Yoongi to see him staring opposite, biting his lip again. He seemed in deep thought about something.

She wanted to ask what was on his mind, as he usually shared these sorts of things with her. But before she could, someone else spoke, "I'm tired, I'm going to sleep." Namjoon yawned as he was walking out of the room.

"How rude, always leaving Jin to take care of the kids," Jimin was humming jokingly as Namjoon left the room.

Jin couldn't help but laugh a bit from his comment due to the others who already were. He picks up a pillow closest to him and chunks it lazily at Jimin, who put his hands up to block it. "Shut up, chim chim." But she could tell he didn't seem to mind that much.

"I'm tired, too," Jungkook was saying as he also rose to his feet. He's about to walk out of the room, but just as he's going to do so he instead turns to Jin, holding his arms out dramatically, "tuck me in, eomma."

Jin had been taking all the jokes rather well today. But this one looked like it made him want to jump off a bridge. Noticing his expression, Jungkook laughs, "Joking, goodnight guys."

She began to feel a bit tired herself. The others were quietly watching TV and having small talk every once in a while, whilst the shifted to get more comfortable.

The fact that she was basically touching Yoongi right now sent goosebumps up her arms. Still trying to get comfortable, he managed to move at the same time she did, his hand gently grazing hers.

As soon as they were both comfortable, still sitting relatively close to each other, he looks to her with wide eyes, "you are really cold."

Her eyes had been on journal that sat in her lap, meeting his chocolate ones instead, "what?" she asks as she snaps out of her gaze.

Yoongi chuckles at her, not saying anything for a moment as he pauses to think. "Come here," he says, and at first she wasn't sure what he meant, until she felt an arm wrap around her shoulder, pulling her into him.

Surprised at his sudden action, she reluctantly laid her head on his chest. Was this meant in a friendly way? Her thoughts were yelling at her, he's just trying to be nice.

Either way, she was definitely warming up. Pulling the blanket a bit further up their bodies again, she tried to focus on the TV, but it ended up being hard for her. This was most likely due to the fact she could hear the pace of his breathe, his chest rising against her. Being this close to him was making her heart skip more beats than she could stand to keep up with. Why did he do this to her?

Eventually, she gave up as she sat there, feeling Yoongi begin to gently rub her arm to help her warm up. Her eyes were growing heavier by the second as she grew more and more tired – no telling what time it even was now.

Trying to stay awake, the guys all soon left the room to go to sleep themselves. It wasn't long until it was just the two of them, sitting in the now dark room as Jin had turned the lights off.

Yoongi's chest was rather comfortable in that moment as her eyes began to force shut. Her body begged for rest and she cuddled a bit further into him, not having control of her actions as she fell into a deep sleep.

The last thing she felt was soft lips pressing against her forehead, and a soft whisper as she fully drifted off, "Goodnight, Katarina."

둘; I remember that moment

"Guys, did you not hear me? I said, breakfast is ready!" Jin trots into the room, a clear lost expression on his face. He'd figured his friends just hadn't heard them, as he knew everyone (including himself) loved food. So, when they had a chance to eat it, why the hell would they ignore it?

As soon as he walks through the doorway into the living room, noticing they're all huddled together. He opens his mouth, trying to understand what they were gawking at. Ever since that first year in university, they were all close friends. It wasn't long into their large friendship that things started to bloom. Not only between Taehyung and Hailey, but Yoongi and Katarina.
The first two had been rather upfront with their feelings from the very first time they even realized they had them. Hailey had boasted about it to her, and she'd encouraged her to tell him how she felt. Turns out, Taehyung had done the exact same thing with the guys, and they ended up confessing to each other on the same day.

Kat and Yoongi on the other hand, not so much. They were both loners, meaning they had not-the-best social skills. And when it came to their feelings, that was something they didn't enjoy sharing unless the other did first.

When he suddenly paused, and she almost pissed herself thinking he realized she was there. But no, he was just restarting it. She was used to seeing him focused while working on music, but he seemed extra focused on this piece, like it really meant something to him.
She listened to the melody again as he replayed it in his headphones, beginning to bob his head. It sounded really lovely to her, and what made it all the much astonishing was when he started rapping along to it.
"If only I had just one day, I want to peacefully fall asleep, intoxicated with your sweet scent. If there's a chance, I want to put my body in your warm deep eyes. I like that, your long straight-" he suddenly cut himself off when he seemed to meet something about it he didn't like.
She felt like she was going to pass out as she could only admire his work. She couldn't believe he'd really wrote that and did the melody. It made her eager to hear the whole song.
Snapping out her gaze on him, she realized she was probably sort of creepy – just standing here, watching him. Scolding herself, she's about to walk out of the room before taking one last glance at the boy she admired.
Only to notice a certain something on his desk beside him, wide open, like he'd been looking at it. Her eyes widen a bit, and she has to squint as if to see if her eyes were right.
They were indeed, there was no other explanation. Her journal.

셋; I looked up to you

Silence again, before she admits to him, too, "I felt the same way."

She practically jumps at this, "Of course I would!"
The smile returns to his lips as he nods, about to turn back to the desk before he poses another question to her. "Who were your lyrics about?"
He had a look on his face that looked like he already knew the answer. She felt a lot better now that they'd confessed to each other, so she let the truth fall off her lips, "you."
"Just wanted to make sure," and with that, he turned, holding onto her hand to drag her to the chairs at his desk.
And there was where they'd be the rest of the night, to finish their song.

"I'm uncomfortable," Namjoon mumbles from the side of the table.
Hailey is quick to speak up at this one, "Why? It's not like you and Jin don't get it on every night."
The entire table burst into laughs, and it was now Jin & Namjoon's turns to cringe.
"Okay, stop, I can't take anymore of this joke," Katarina says as she looks to her two friends that looked like they actually wanted to die. She couldn't help but giggle a bit at their expressions herself though.
The nine friends continued their breakfast in silence. Some of them finished earlier than others, and headed back to their rooms to prepare for the 'big day.'
Soon, the only ones left at the table were Jimin, Hailey, and Katarina. Yoongi had just left to go get ready, but just before he'd left the room he'd caught the corner of her eye, sending her one of those cute smiles.
Her cheeks heated up from the sudden attention, and she shyly grinned before he disappeared down the hall. Snapping her head back to her plate, she continues to eat her dinner, hoping neither of them noticed.
But it wasn't long until she felt a gaze she knew too well on her, and she knew for a fact she'd failed. She tried to ignore Hailey's knowing stare, but it was something she'd always found rather difficult – because one thing about Hails was she did not fucking give up.
Eventually she felt it burning through her skull, and finally whipped her head up, slight annoyance pinging in her tone, "what?!"
At this, her best friend seems taken aback a bit as she puts a fake expression of surprise on her face, holding a hand to her heart. "Excuse me," she hums, before leaning her elbows on the table to get closer, "did you two little love birds finally confess?"
She didn't really care very much if anyone knew at this point, but there was no reason she shouldn't try to have fun with it. "Why do you think that?" She raises a brow.
Hailey scoffs, taking her elbows off the table to instead lean back in the chair she sat on, "Oh, shut up, don't act like you and Yoongi weren't eyeballing each other this entire morning."
The thought of everything that had happened between her and Yoongi caused a smile to spread across her lips, and she suddenly didn't feel like playing around anymore. "Yeah, maybe we did," she admits, looking down to her plate.
Jimin pipes up from beside Hails, "Really, are you guys together?" He sounded more worried than he did anything else, which confused her. She decided not to think much of it, he was probably just nervous about their audition.
Katarina shakes her head no as a reply, and Hailey frowns, "Seriously – he didn't ask you either? Why are guys so slow?" It was clear she was a bit sad that Taehyung still hadn't asked her out yet as she diverted her eyes to the ceiling. Pushing those emotions away, she speaks happily again, "I'm glad you guys finally stopped being such pussies, though."
She could only giggle, "Me too."
Hours later, it was time to leave. The Big Hit studios were located in the city, which they most definitely did not live in. By city, she meant big city – as in two to three hours away (depending who drove.)
It'd taken everyone a bit, but soon they were all ready with the things needed for their small trip and everything. They'd all shuffled out of the house, and were about to all climb in the suburban when Jin spoke up, stopping them.
"Can you guys fit four in one of the rows? I hate driving for so long being cramped together," he's saying as he opens the drivers side.
They all exchange glances of disbelief. Yoongi rolls his eyes as he opens the back door to climb back to his spot, figuring he wouldn't be involved, "I swear, Jin, you're like an actual mother sometimes."
Jin was already situated in his seat, and soon Yoongi was too. The tall boy glared back at his friend, "I'm sorry, did you want to drive?"
He only shrugs in reply, leaning back in his seat and going on his phone as he states cockily, "I could."
"It's fine," Namjoon is saying as everyone begins to climb in the car, trying to figure out how to make Jin's request work, "Hailey can just—" He stopped talking when he witnessed something that changed the statement he'd been making.
Katarina had been mid-climbing into the back to sit by Yoongi, like always. She and everyone else already knew what Namjoon was going to say, and they just figured that was most likely what was going to happen. Cause what else would? But just as she's turning in the cramped back row of the car to sit down, a strong force is applied against her, pushing her backwards right onto Yoongi's lap.
Everyone who had been looking back eyes widened, as they were unaware about how to react to this situation. The culprit was no one other than Hailey, an evil smirk on her face as she hurriedly took Katarina's previous spot, pulling Taehyung to sit beside her in the third seat.
"There!" She hums to the front of the car, "we're situated!"
Katarina had feel her cheeks practically burning off her face, and she was horrified to see Yoongi's expression. She didn't know if he was okay with this or not. Not to mention the other looks the guys were giving.
Jin hadn't even looked back at the commotion, simply just started the car and began to pull out of the driveway. Her, on the other hand, had no idea how she was going to pull off sitting in Min Yoongi's lap for three hours. What the hell was Hailey thinking?
"Wait—" She tries to say, but this time what stopped her wasn't her best friend.
She feels his arms wrap around her waist, and he tightens his grip. "It's okay," she hears his voice, causing her to stop everything she was doing.
"Okay," is all she can say, her heart beating too fast and her brain thinking of too many things.
She was definitely embarrassed to be seen in such a position with the boy she liked, but other than that it wasn't like she hated it. Who the hell could hate being like this with Min Yoongi? She answered her own question a second later with the following thought; absolutely no one.
So they sat like that – for the next three hours.
"Can't you play something someone actually fucking likes?!" Hailey was complaining as an Ed Sheeran song came on over the radio, that was too loud for her liking.
They'd just entered the city, and the thought that in only minutes they'd be in front of Big Hit Studios had everyone rather jumpy. Not Hailey so much it seemed, since she was currently complaining about what was being played on the radio, out of all things.
"Can't you just shut the fuck up?" Hoseok turns to look in the back and playfully retorts to see her reaction. He already knew it would be hilarious, and them messing around with each other was something to calm their nerves.
Annoyance spreads clear over her features, "Are you trying to throw down, or?"
"Yeah, dance battle as soon as we get there," he challenges, neither of them being serious, obviously.
Jin is just turning a corner as the two continue bickering. You could tell they were getting closer and closer to the studios, and the aura in the car started the get tenser by the second.
"If you guys don't shut up, I'm going to shove the hot packs I brought up your asses when we get there," the elderly is heard from the front.
Some of them burst into laughter. And Jimin's confused voice is heard, "What – hyung, why did you bring hot packs?"
He didn't answer – because in that moment, they pulled into a particular parking lot. Jimin didn't push him to answer either as gasps were heard from all the friends.
Everyone was putting their faces against the windows to look up at the large building. No one could quite believe it, they were here, at Big Hit Studios. It was one of the largest in South Korea, and they were right in front of it.
It took him a while to find a spot as everyone started nervously chatting about their audition. Hailey and Katarina stood quiet to let the guys talk it all over.
Soon, they were all climbing the car. Katarina was one of the last ones, and once she was standing – she firstly could barely feel her legs. After getting the feeling back, she stands by her friends to look up at the building they were about to walk in, seeing lots of other excited young people their age rushes inside also.
"Holy shit, we're really doing this," Namjoon's voice is heard in disbelief.
They all slowly began their walk through the parking lot, the only conversation being about how crazy this was to them.
"God, this place is huge, do you guys know where to go?" Hailey is asking as they get closer, the nerves only growing with each step.
Katarina let her eyes fall onto Yoongi that walked beside her. He'd been completely silent, which was normal for him, but not this silent. Everyone knew he usually liked to add in some rude comments, but he hadn't even bothered since they'd got here and most of the ride here.
Panicked thoughts rushed into her head, and she was fighting to gain the courage to speak up to him. Part of her didn't understand why she was still having so much unexplainable trouble with it.
When he suddenly looks to the guys, "Can I have a solo part – for the audition?"
They all look back at him whilst continuing walking like he was mentally insane. None of them could believe the words that'd just come out of his mouth, including herself as she stared at him with wide eyes.
"Dude, no, that's cutting our plan," V tells him from beside Hailey, actually being serious for once. This was how you knew something was important. When the determined look on Yoongi's face doesn't change, he looks to his hyungs in horror for assistance.
Namjoon looks back to the front as he orders, "No, that's not part of the plan." Jin only nodded in agreement.
At the fact his friends didn't agree, Yoongi heaved out a disappointed sigh. Her eyes were stuck on him, but he didn't notice. What had he been planning? She wondered as she watched him pat his pockets as if he was searching for something.
In a split moment, the disappointment is wiped off his face once he seems to find whatever he was in search for. Looking back to the guys who hadn't noticed anything, he just says, "Alright, nevermind then."
Min Yoongi, what are you planning?

다섯; I didn't know your significance back then
After the guys had signed in, the energy being spread throughout the friend group was hectic. As they walked down the halls, it was hard for any of them to contain themselves. But there was strict rules and security saying that if you couldn't or went wandering somewhere, you'd get banned from the company – so none of them did those things.
They all walked together, trying to calm themselves. Katarina was doing alright as she walked closer to Yoongi, as all of them were squished together. Her green eyes trailed over all the areas they'd passed that belonged to famous idols.
A lot of them she recognized, and some she surprisingly didn't. There were whispers spreading through the nine friends, until Hailey blurted rather loudly, "oh my god."
Their heads all whip to her in confusion. She's holding her pointer finger as a certain sign that hung.
SEVENTEEN
Nervous glances from her friends were shot right at Katarina. They expected her to explode right then and there as they stood right before the sign. She tried to contain her excitement as she let her eyes look down the hall. She could only imagine the same thirteen boys walking down the same halls she currently walked on.
She wanted so badly to let out a deathly scream, but there were security guards right there. The others had to shove her a little towards the direction they were walking before she could finally move again.
Once they were away from the security guards, she let out a high pitched squeal of excitement that she'd been holding in.
"I expected that a lot sooner," Hoseok hums to ease the mood.
Hailey nudges her shoulder, "Just imagine Joshua walking down these same floors," she motions to the ground, and Katarina let's her eyes linger on it as they walk. She'd ever mentioned her favorite member.
"Shut up, you're going to make her make a run down the hall screaming for him," Jin looks back disapprovingly.
Taehyung starts giggling, "Jin-hyung, don't be silly, she only does that for Yoong—" he couldn't even say the last syllable in the boy's name before he was being slapped on the arm by no one other than well, Min Yoongi. The impact causes a girly "ow!" to leave Tae's lips as he rubs his arm.
He looks to Hailey for some sort of help, but she shrugs, "you sort of deserved that one."
They walked for what felt like forever, until the sound of lots of people were heard. They soon approached a long line standing in the hall, everyone holding slips with numbers on them. The number indicated your turn, and everyone that was auditioning had gotten one when they'd checked in.
The boys all had the number 474 attached as a sticker on their shirts. Katarina let her eyes linger over the line they stood in. It didn't seem that long, but still, there was no telling how long they'd be waiting here.
Looking back to the boys, they were tense. She found herself wondering what they were even planning to do for the audition, as she had never been listening whilst they were discussing it.
She wanted to ask now, but they looked so tense she decided not to. It would only make them more nervous, and that was the last thing she wanted.
"You guys are going to kill it, stop looking like you're about to attend a funeral," Hailey speaks up about half an hour later. The line had moved up faster than expected, making her wonder if they were just denying people half way through their auditions or something.
The thought worried her a bit. She didn't want to see her best friends heart broken over this.
They all send their friend a thankful smile, but no words left their lips due to them being in deep thought. Most likely, they were going over whatever they planned to do in their heads repeatedly, making sure they did it all perfectly.
Moments and moments passed, the line going up more. Most of the guys were pretty nervous, even Namjoon, who kept reassuring his friends they'd do fine.
Katarina couldn't help but watch as people left the room. A very small amount of them ran out jumping around happily, meaning they'd most likely got positive results. The company didn't just accept people here. Your audition got recorded, then watched by everyone at the company. That was just if they liked it though – then the decision was made if you were let in or not. There, you'd begin as a trainee.
Being an idol was a lot of work. Which was why she'd never see herself doing anything so silly, she much preferred to just sit in her room and write music.
Most people, anyways, came out looking rather sad, some even in tears. It was common for the company staffs to be rather harsh, and you could tell that was definitely the case by people's expressions as they left.
This only made the boys a bit more nerve wrecked as it moved up again. Their eyes fall on the realization that they were standing right at the doorway. They were next.
Katarina and Yoongi are standing towards the back, and he was practically shaking, which she could tell due to how close they were forced to stand in the crowded halls. This causes her to look up at him, biting her lip as she notices his worried expression. It was clear he was trying to hide it, but she saw right through him. She knew Yoongi didn't really see himself as some sort of god, although he should.
She didn't think much of it in that second. All she wanted was for him to calm down as she reaches out and grabs his hand. The action causes him to jump a bit at the sudden touch, and he looks confused until he looks down to the small girl that stood beside him.
Katarina sends him an innocent smile, and he glances down at their hands. Meeting her eyes again, he intertwines their fingers, squeezing her hand a bit as if he knew what she was trying to tell him by the action.
"Next!" The word is called from inside as the previous auditionees left the room. The guys all exchange looks, knowing they were next, as if asking each other telepathically – are we really doing this?
"You're gonna do great," she whispers to Yoongi when his friends begin to pile inside the room. Eyes are on them as he looks down at her. Hailey had stayed back as the others entered, and Katarina figured they weren't allowed to go inside the room unless they were auditioning themselves.
The boy before her glances inside the room, where his friends were looking at him impatiently, before back to her. He has to think for a moment, before keeping a grip on her hand, and pulling her inside with him. This caught her and Hailey both off guard, as her best friend follows them inside also.
"I can't do this without you here," she hears him mumble as his hand leaves hers, and he walks to the middle of the room where his friends stood in front of the staff.
Her cheeks flush, and the staff look to the two girls standing there. A weird expression is on their faces, and one of them glances from Yoongi to her for a moment. It's silent, and you could tell the boys were nervous as they await the command to begin the audition.
The camera was rolling, she noticed when someone was holding it up behind them. One of the staffs clear their throat, "So you're a group you've formed yourselves?" Is the first thing they ask.
They exchange more glances. "Yes, we're called Bangtan Sonyeondan," Namjoon speaks up after, voicing his out rather professionally.
The staffs are all nodding but they didn't seem like they cared very much. "And what do you all do?" They were asking after the seven of them all introduced themselves.
It was quiet for another moment. The two girls on the sidelines were curious of this themselves. Or at least Katarina was, being that she hadn't heard much at all about the group they'd formed.
They'd all introduced who rapped and who sang. As she watched her friends, she noticed that their roles seemed to just fit them. They also mentioned they'd practiced dance, which seemed to intrigue the staff a bit. But when they'd shared that Yoongi had wrote the song, it'd intrigued them even more.
Everyone looked to the boy once the information was shared, and one of the staff rose a brow as they ask, "Is that true? You write music?"
He nods slowly, "Yeah, it's my hobby."
They all nod in unison, seemingly interested now. "Well, let's hear it." The guys all look to Yoongi as he takes a disc out of his pocket to hand to one of the staffs to play.
He does so, and they're quick to play the disc from the speakers. Katarina listened as the beat filled her ears, sounding very upbeat. She could tell it was one of the many projects Yoongi had been working on when a small smile plays on his lips as it begins.
They all get into some sort of formation. There was an expression on their faces like they'd been practicing this for a lifetime.
There was a certain smirk on Yoongi's face as he seemed to gain some sort of confidence she didn't know he'd had right then. He was in the middle of the formation as he began.
"At first, I was only curious as I started to show interest in you. Holy shhh, yeah, even if you ignore me, you'll fall for me in a minute." They really had choreo to go with the song. Hailey looks to her with a surprised look, clearly thinking the same thing she was – they were good.
"We look good together, without you, I'm like a Seoul city without lights. I fiercely glare at your empty spot, a rabbit hole graffiti. Without you, my days are like a tragedy."
Yoongi's verse ends, and he throws a glance her way. She was so surprised as they danced, perfectly in sync almost, that she barely caught it. A smile formed on her lips as she watched her friends, realizing more with each minute how much this really, really meant to them all.
"Us meeting isn't just a coincidence, meeting you was what I wanted," the song continued. She was so focused on her friends that she forgot the staff were even there.
Looking to them, their reactions were – priceless. Some of them were even clapping along to the beat of the song. Hailey starts clapping with them, the excitement riling her up also. Katarina gives her a weird look, as if to ask what the fuck are you doing but her best friend grabs the girl's hands, forcing her to start clapping too.
The song continued, and the two of them felt rather proud. They'd never believed in their friends more than they did in that moment.
When it ended, they erupted into cheers of happiness. The staff seemed rather impressed, as they also began to clap. The boys bow in unison, large smiles on their faces as they all stand, breathing hard from the dance, and stare at the staff expectantly.
The nine friends watch as they all turn to exchange words with each other, before looking back to everyone. The one in the middle who'd asked all the questions smiled, holding up a stack of papers, "Please fill these out, and we'll look into accepting you into Big Hit Studios."
This didn't mean they were accepted – this was just a maybe. But either way, it caused the boys to jump in excitement. They all high-five and hug each other before rushing to each individually fill out the papers.
The girls stay put, trying to contain themselves. But it was no lie they were extremely happy for their friends, too.
"I can't believe this is really happening," Katarina mumbles to Hailey as she holds a hand to her head, letting out a sigh of disbelief. Part of her was overwhelmed.
Soon, they'd filled out the papers, and it was time for them to leave and await a possible response from the company. There was no clue how long it would take, but they were told they'd get back to them as soon as possible.
The nine of them were all jumpy and happy as they left the large studio building. Hailey jumps on Tae's back, and he begins to give her a piggyback ride as she squeals, "you guys seriously did that shit!"
Katarina nods, agreeing with her friend as she looks to them all, mainly Yoongi, "yeah, the song was really good, so was you guys' dancing!"
"I made up the choreo!" Hoseok calls from the front, just as their reaching the suburban.
Everyone is climbing in, lots of conversation was happening when Jungkook adds to what Hoseok had said, "Hey, I helped with the choreo!"
Namjoon glances back at all the commotion from the front. "Yeah, but the song was all thanks to our man Yoongi," he states. Everyone nods vigorously in agreeance, all eyes falling on the boy that sat in the back, not to mention the girl that sat uncomfortably on his lap.
Jin still insisted he have the middle seat of the front free.

여섯 ; back then I was content with just looking at you
Katarina sits quietly at her usual spot on the sofa, much unlike the rest of her friends except Yoongi who were all jumping around to the music they had booming over the stereo. Ever since they'd gotten home, they'd been like this, crazily dancing and drinking like there was no tomorrow. It was clear they were happy with the outcome of their audition.
Although it wasn't like they even got accepted, and deep down they didn't expect to. But either way, they'd believed they did well, and so had the staffs. They'd worked hard, and whether they got accepted or not, it'd already paid off to them.
That, required a celebration.
Her, however, wasn't too much in the mood for drinking and celebrating. She was proud of the boys, yes, but there were too many thoughts that clouded her head for her to be up, jumping like a crazy person.
She kept wondering about her and Yoongi's song, and how he'd asked to perform solo even despite the guys plans. It was all – weird to her.
Part of her almost wished she would have showed that song to the staffs. That was how proud she was of it, although Yoongi had done most of the work. The fact that it was even partly written by him only made her love it more. The thought of them sitting in his studio all night, side by side as they wrote what they were passionate about – each other – caused a goofy smile to spread across her lips. Tuning out the music that played in her ears and her friends yelling, she places her chin in the palm of her hand, gazing up at the ceiling dearingly as she daydreamed.
She suddenly feels a presence in front of her, and a stare she figured was Hailey's. However, when she looks up, she saw her best friend dancing with Taehyung, laughter exploding from their lips. He was staring down at her with heart eyes as he grabbed her hand, twirling her around and letting her droop before he dramatically caught her, leaning down with her to look deeply into her eyes. It looked like some sort of cheesy romance movie scene, but she couldn't deny how cute the two were together.
Wait, so who is it then? She snaps out of her trance, whipping her head up. This time, she'd hoped it was Yoongi – but, her green eyes instead locked with Hoseok's.

She gives them a blank stare, "I hate you guys."

She thinks back to the way Yoongi pulled off such a cool vibe whenever he did such. How the hell he did that? She had no idea, but maybe she should let loose. After all, what did she really have to worry about anymore?
Other than the fact she & Hailey have class tomorrow.
But that was the last thing on any of their minds, and by the looks of Hailey then, they most likely weren't going to attend.
A groan leaves her lips as she rises from the sofa, causing surprised looks to spread across her friends faces as she hums, "Alright, I'm in."

"Uh – is Kat gonna rap?" Jimin asked innocently as he notices the girl, who steps out to be in clear view, standing beside Kookie. Everyone looked rather confused.
She nods with a shrug, "they asked me so they could make fun of me."

Katarina is chuckling at the two. She knew this was going to go awfully, but it was just for fun anyways.

This isn't my first time rapping," he began to stumble a bit, trying to find the words to say, "it's different now, I'm walking along the beat," Hoseok continued his beatboxing. Everyone was snickering every once in a while at their facial expressions. "I cover them all during the summer, then I catch them all. Jungkook, look at me, look at me!" He finishes, yelling the last part, before raising his arms in the air and walking forward to his hyungs who patted him on the back.

I'm the hip-hop that Gwangju gave birth to," everyone started whistling at his words, but he didn't look too done yet, "This is the start to Jeolla-do's rap, I'll shake you up go burst. 'Cause I'm really smashing!" He finished dramatically with a bow, and everyone burst into laughter, clapping a bit too.
Katarina for some reason felt pressured despite the fact this was all a joke. She cleared her throat as the two boys began to beatbox for her, trying not to giggle as she thought of what to rap.
It was obvious she loved to write music, but she definitely wasn't one for free-styling. As she stood there under her friend's gazes, she realized this.
Then it hit her, a really, really silly idea. Not to mention she didn't know what else to do in her current situation. She clears her throat, about to begin and rap Yoongi's part to their song because she had no other ideas, when a voice is heard behind them, causing the commotion to stop.
Hoseok and Jungkook went from having the time of their lives with their little 'beat boxing session,' to looking completely terrified at Yoongi's sudden presence. The dark haired boy walks further into the room as he says, "Guys, this is rude, we all know Kat can't rap."
The sudden insult causes the small girl who had just about to have attempted to – as the boys would put it – spit some bars, pouts as she looks up. He now stood beside her, a playful, cocky smirk on his lips. Yoongi only glanced down at her pouting face, and he send her a smile, followed by a wink. His sudden cocky attitude had her heart pumping out of her chest, and she couldn't deny that the sight of him acting this way was hot.
Suddenly, she didn't even care about the fact he'd insulted her. It was most likely true that she couldn't rap, even though she'd never tried – and Yoongi was joking. Now if anything, she was more intrigued to know what he was about to do.
"I'll take her spot," Yoongi hums an offer. Though it really wasn't much of an offer as he wasn't going to let the boys deny him.
