Hailey chuckles from beside Taehyung, who wasn't paying attention to anything that was happening. The childish boy instead was just playing with strands of her hair, in his own world. "You guys just wanted to bully her," she joins in to the joking session.
"That's not true!" Jungkook cries defensively, unaware that everyone was kidding.
Everyone starts laughing after this, confusing the poor maknae a bit. Hoseok then looks to Yoongi, who was standing there patiently, "Okay, let's hear it."
The two silly boys begin to give him a beat. And everyone is staring at Yoongi expectantly, extremely curious of what he was about to do. Despite his friends gazes, he didn't look nervous at all for once.
"My name is Y-O-O-N-G-I. Other rappers are all behind me, same as always. I tease my tongue this way and that over this beat – all your rap makes me sleepy," at this point, it was like he was singing some sort of actual song. She wondered if this was even a freestyle as everyone began to clap along, "Shall we rewind the clip? Our music will make you cry. The name is Bangtan. What's coming out of your mouth right now is – exclamation?!" When he finished he did a bow as they all started clapping.
She'd never seen him so cocky and happy before. This was all she could think as he laughed at their reactions. He never smiled like that. They really must be happy about their audition.
Part of her was worried. Despite the fact the boys didn't apparently mind too much whether they got accepted or not, since it was about a 1 out of a 100 chance; she still knew they'd be heartbroken if they didn't. They believed they were good enough – she believed they were good enough.
They deserved this. This was their dream, and they were really following it. And seeing them so happy over this, she realized as she watched them all jump around, trying to decide the winner of the 'rap battle' – was that she should've never doubted them in the first place.
일곱; I neglected you when I once yearned for you so
She decided to force herself to attend class the next day.
This was only because she remembered she had important tests in a few subjects, not to mention an English Lit. project she had to turn in, which she'd done the day after she got it. It was completely reasonable to say Katarina was a bit of a dork. As unlike Hailey, who had very clearly decided to skip due to the crazy night they'd had, Katarina didn't miss classes. It was a rare occasion for her, and she even liked to attend when she was sick.
So she managed to push herself through all her classes that Monday. It wasn't like she had anything to drink last night, so she wasn't hungover. She was just very sleep deprived. And as she walked out of the main college building that afternoon, after her last class had ended, she felt like she was going to pass out right onto the pavement.
Heaving her bag a bit further up her shoulder, she put a hand to her head as if to soothe herself. Something had happened to her when she got no sleep was she'd get indescribably dizzy. Her vision would start to blur, and she'd see spots occasionally. As a child, she struggled a lot with bad eating and sleeping habits. Due to them, she'd always had these sort of effects throughout her youth.
Deciding she didn't have the energy to go to the guys house, she used all her strength to get to her dorm. She was gaining a few looks from people as she walked past them, but she never met their gazes due to the fact her eyes remained on the ground.
She hadn't felt so dizzy in a while, and the sudden lost feeling was driving her insane. Although it was a horrible idea, she sped up her pace, eager to just get to her dorm and collapse onto her bed.
Her phone vibrating in the back of her pocket causes her to slow down a bit. She ended up stumbling as she felt for her phone in her back pocket, eventually pulling it out.
She turns on the screen, her vision blurring again a bit. Squinting, she managed to read the message.
Genius Producer: Hey, are you at your dorm yet? I'm coming by.
Genius Producer: And if you're wondering why, it's cause I miss you. Watching Taehyung and Hailey all day made me gag.
Genius Producer: Since you went to class, I didn't have anyone to gag with
It took her longer than normal to read the messages due to her awful vision. Trying to manage walking at the same time, she holds the phone in a way, so she could begin to type back.
Although this seemed to become to much for her exhausted body. Her eyes began to grow heavy, and she felt her skin grow wet. Trying to calm herself as she began to freak out, she realized she was growing closer to her dorm. Almost there.
Suddenly, she feels the sudden impact of running into another person. The entire time she'd still been staring down at her phone, her thumbs hovering over the open keyboard, but she'd typed no words.
That impact seemed to be enough as she stumbled back. If her body hadn't been giving up then, it definitely was now. The dizziness ultimately took over as she stumbled, and she felt her will give out as everything turned black. Gasps were heard around her as the small girl collapsed to the ground, out cold.

아홉; Even then I didn't know your significance

She didn't turn to face Yoongi nor watch him leave as his footsteps were heard quickly down the hall, probably to go tell the others. Her brain was aching at this point as she thought over and over about what Hobi had just told her.
You guys can just ignore the ban.
The more the sentence burned itself into her brain, the more she didn't even have to think about what he was talking about. The ban, the industry they were working for had a ban on dating. What else would he have meant?
It hurt her to turn and meet his eyes, but she did. Slowly but surely, she looked into Yoongi's glass, brown eyes, that were piling with tears that he fought back. 
"There's really a ban?" her voice cracks mid sentence as she breaks down completely. Now everything was really catching up to her. They were all leaving, she would practically never see them, rarely hear from them. Now her and Yoongi couldn't even be together in the first place.
He slowly nods, biting his lips as he tries to process what to say. She didn't wait for him to do such a thing as the tears began to fall rapidly from her eyes, she began to walk at a fast pace, pushing right past him and beginning her way quickly down the hall. 
How could she be so stupid? Everyone knew the k-pop industries weren't the 'free-est' when it came to their trainees and eventually idols. But there were really things as silly as dating bans? She had never payed attention to the media and such to know any sort of insanity like that. It blew her mind. They really just deny people who decide to work for them any sort of relationship like that? 
She was walking so quickly down the hall, her mind spinning. With each step she took, she felt like falling onto the ground and just sinking into the floor to never been seen again more and more. Her heart was shattered, and she couldn't stop the tears from pouring from her eyes like rapid waterfall. 
Everything had come together just to crumble. She should've never supported them on this, was the first thing she thought, but would that make her selfish?
The worst part about it all was that they all knew. They all knew when they signed those contracts that day at the studio. They knew they would have to move away, they knew there was a ban. And they'd signed them anyway. Which wasn't the bad part.
The bad part was they had kept it from the girls for so long.
Her pent up sadness began to turn into anger as she walked. She didn't even know what was happening anymore. It was a mix of pure anger and complete, utter, depression. 
She's just about to reach the stairs, desperate to just get back to her dorm more than anything. She knew she shouldn't of skipped class today, but then again, she wouldn't of found this out. 
Just as her foot is on the first step from the top, a hand grips her wrist from behind, yanking her back towards them. A squeal of surprise leaves her lips as she stumbles back a bit, barely being able to process the current event as she falls back into the arms of the boy she'd been running from. 
Her heartbeat had accelerated from the fact she'd almost fell there because of him. This had caused her to sit there in surprise for a moment, so much that she hadn't even heard Yoongi's words as he desperately stared down at her, repeating them over and over.
"Can you listen to me?"
There was a sense of desperation in his voice. She nor anyone else in the world had never heard Min Yoongi speaking in such a way. 
But that didn't phase her, at least not then. Not in that moment with all the remorse she was currently feeling.
Not to mention, she was incapable of thinking straight anymore.
As soon as she wakes up from her trance, she rushes to get out of his grip, stepping a few steps away from him. His eyes were sad when he looked to her, but you could tell he was trying not to show how sad he was. That was just Yoongi's personality, which she hadn't noticed much back in the restroom. He always tried to show strength, like he didn't care about anything -- even when he cared so badly.
Meeting his eyes, a trillion memories hit her in the face. It all made her heart hurt more along with the realization they couldn't be together. 
The anger shoots up her spine as she narrows her eyes, spouting in disbelief, "how could you keep that from me for so long?" she furrows her brows as she stares up at the boy, waiting for a reply.
A frustrated sigh leaves his lips as he diverts his eyes to the ceiling. "What did you want me to do? I didn't know about it until I saw the papers that we had to sign. Did you want me to stand up to them and say, oh I'm sorry, I can't sign this, never mind? I couldn't do that, I couldn't back out," he runs a hand through his hair over and over as he explained, "there was no way I could avoid that."
She'd stopped crying through the small encounter, but as she looked up at him it made her tear up all over again. They hadn't even been official yet. And as she stared up at him, she could tell he was having trouble doing that whole 'show strength' thing he always did. 
He was hurt just as much as her.
Suddenly, it hurt too much to look at him. Forcing herself to look to the ground as the tears begin to fall rapidly, she could barely make out the words, "I wanted you to tell me we couldn't be together." 
No amount of pain she'd experienced in her life could amount to how she felt right then. 
It hurt so immensely, it was hard for her to not sob. Yoongi could only stare at the broken girl before him that he liked so badly. The thought that he'd done this to her made him want to punch the wall and many more things. It was clear he wasn't good at these sorts of things despite his many talents. He hadn't known what to do.
Stepping forward towards the girl that had taken many steps away from him, she's still looking at the ground, the tears visible as they fell to the floor under her. Slowly, he places his finger under her chin to make her look up at him. She reluctantly let him as he came even closer to cup her cheeks, raising his thumbs to gently wipe the tears from her soft skin. 
She tried to stop the tears as she met his pretty brown eyes that she loved so much. In fact, there wasn't a singular thing she didn't love about Yoongi. All of his qualities were positive to her. Even the fact that he liked to sleep over anything else and could for days. There was nothing negative about this boy in her eyes. 
"I didn't tell you because I couldn't take seeing you like this, I don't want you to be hurt," his voice is low as he continues to wipe away any tears that dared to fall from her glassy green eyes, "I don't want that to exist to us, I still want to be with you."
Part of her wanted to kiss him, to agree with him, to tell him they could work through this, they could ignore it. That part of her so badly wanted to do all of those things, and was pushing her to do so. 
But the other part of her forced herself to think of them. She couldn't think of herself anymore. This was for their futures, not for her own selfishness. Her and Yoongi being together would be dangerous, it wasn't allowed. They were just starting their careers, they'd almost done it, they were following their dream. 
The thought of her ruining all of what they were working for would break her more than this, she realized. And she couldn't let that happen.
"But you can't," she tries to sound strong as she says this. She tries to hide the fact that everything inside of her was aching. "We can't be together, Yoongi."
As the words fall from her lips she stepped back to release herself from his grip. His hands fell to his side as he took in everything she'd just said to him as he felt his heart shatter in his chest. His mouth was slightly agape in surprise that she'd said such.
His brown eyes linger on her as she begins to go down the steps, to leave him here. 
"Kat!" He calls as he begins to go after her, before she stops on the step she was currently on. 
She didn't let herself look at him. She couldn't. She knew that if she met his eyes it would only hurt more, it would only tempt her more to stay. And for the boys and for Yoongi, she knew she couldn't stay.
"I want you to follow your dream, Yoongi," it took all of her to send him the small smile she threw his way, still not meeting his eyes, "I accept that I can't be included in it."
With that, she left, her bag that included all of the things she'd kept at their house over her shoulder. She didn't know when they were leaving, but she told herself she couldn't come back here as it was probably soon. 
She made sure to be quiet as she slipped outside onto the porch. As soon as she was in the front yard, she walked a bit faster, all the way to the curb. Praying that no one saw her, she turned in the tall, green grass that the boys never mowed, to look up at the house she had so many memories in. 
As much as she tried to not cry anymore, she couldn't help it as she looked up at the house. Were they selling it? she wondered, probably. 
She knew she needed to talk to Hailey, and she would message the rest of the guys, too. She wasn't sure if she would stay in touch with them or not, but one thing she was aware of, was that she couldn't talk to Yoongi. She knew talking to him would only put her through more pain, not to mention the pain he was in. Neither of them needed that.
Finally, she turns and begins her walk back to her college dorm.
 To think that what she'd always wanted to badly had been right in front of her, only to crumble like dead leaves.

열여섯; I remember when I first met you
Hailey runs a hand through her pink hair as she adjusts the bag on her shoulder, chewing her favorite flavor of gum as she walks down the hall of the college she attended, (she still asks herself how in the world she actually got in it in the first place.) She was late to her last class of the day, not to mention how she'd skipped all the others she'd had that day. 
This was a common occurrence with her. It wasn't that she purposely did it. It was just that she got distracted doing other things - like, not attending class by simply sleeping instead. 
She was basically the complete opposite of her best friend. Maybe that was why they worked so well together, she thought as she brainlessly scrolled through her instagram feed. 
At this point, she was only steps away from being in class, that her best friend, Katarina, was in also. Minutes and minutes passed as she found herself glancing everywhere around the lifeless halls, heaving out a sigh of frustration. Why was she taking so long? She needed food.
The sound of a door opening causes her head to jerk that way in excitement. She'd expected her eyes to meet the green orbs of her best friend, but instead, she was greeted with two boys who had come out of a completely different class, she'd realized. 
This had caused her to groan again in frustration as she went back to leaning against the wall in pure boredom. Her noise of complaint caused the two boys to notice her standing there carelessly  as they began to walk down the hall together.
She didn't pay much attention as she was just in her own head, but she could feel a pair of eyes on her. However, she didn't meet them. 
As they grew closer, she began to be able to hear their conversation, which wasn't one with much intellectual, to say the least.

"They really aren't, they're about as bad if not worse," the other boy he's walking with replied. His tone practically screamed 'I don't care about anything.' It reminded her a lot of herself. Well, except he actually attended a class, and she only did that every like, other week.
A sigh of annoyance is heard from the other boy meant towards his friend. What the fuck kind of idiotic conversation were they even having? 
"Okay, listen to this," the deep voice clears his throat, "what kind of shoes does a pedophile wear?"

"White vans!" he yelled rather loudly, causing it to echo through the entire hall, before he starts to hysterically laugh at himself and his awful joke. She rethought what he'd just said over, before realizing just how awfully stupid it was herself. 
It was so bad it made her laugh a bit. Plus, the sound of this mystery boy's cute laugh was making her want to laugh even more. 
They heard her laughing as she felt eyes on her. This surprises her a bit as she hurriedly looks to the ground, trying to not make eye contact as it'd be a bit awkward since she didn't even know them. 
"See? She found it funny," she hears the deep voice cry. He was talking about her.
She bit her lip as she so badly wanted to look up and say something. 
Just as she was about to, the sound of a feminine voice is heard coming from somewhere behind them, calling down the hall, "YAH, Hailey!" Her head jerks up, catching a glimpse of the two boys again before falling on her best friend that was running towards her.
Katarina hadn't even acknowledged the guys as she had ran past them, her bag bouncing on her back as she stopped, "did you not hear me the thirty other times I called you?"
She shrugs as she meets her green eyes, "Guess not." 
Hailey tried to pay attention to her friend as she spoke, but her eyes kept getting distracted. The boy with the deep voice kept glancing at her as he and his friend walked. It was no lie when she said he was gorgeous with a capital G, it had her rather surprised as she was unable to take his eyes off of him. How could someone be so pretty but act like a complete child? She loved that.

She cuts herself off when she looks up to see Hailey wasn't even listening to her in the first place due to the trance she was in, staring at something behind them.
Her brows furrow as she stares for a second longer and her best friend that was stuck in some sort of trance. She calls her out here to go get food and now it looked like she just did cocaine, she thought as she slowly turns to figure out what the hell she was even looking at.
Before them, she sees practically a mirror except instead it's two guys. Two boys that were no doubt their age, a bit taller were standing only feet away. One had caramel locks and chocolate eyes, and he stood there in some sort of trance much like Hailey. No way, she thought to herself, they were actually standing there looking at each other. Did they realize how stupid they look? 
She scoffs, they're lucky no one else was here.
That's when her eyes fell on the boy that stood beside the caramel-haired one. His hair was jet black, and he had bangs cut all the way across his forehead that almost covered his eyes. Just barely you could see them, though, with his deep brown orbs that weren't looking back at her, but however at his friend as he called to him. 
Her green eyes looked at his apparel. His sense of style was something she found herself liking a lot. There was nothing better than a guy who dressed well.
"Yah, Taehyung, you idiot. Snap out of your trance, just because a girl actually laughed at your awful joke," the black haired boy is saying as he pushes the other's shoulder.
She forces her eyes off of the two to look back to Hailey. A sigh leaves her lips as she raised her hand to harshly pinch the girl beside her. This caused a bright reaction as a high pitched "ow, what the fuck!" leaved her lips and she looks at Katarina in annoyance.
"You're an idiot," is all the small girl says to her in that 'know it all' tone of hers.

Just as she is, her green eyes meet the dark haired boy's, and her heart almost stopped for a second at how pretty he was. But she told herself she wasn't going to do what Hailey just had. 
The sudden eye contact scared her a bit as she walked faster. It wasn't long until Hailey began to follow after her, "Yah, what the hell?"
It didn't take long before she was walking beside her. "Why are you walking away? Did you not see those hot guys?!"
Katarina stops in her tracks to wrinkle her nose at her friend. "I'm here to go to college, not to get dick," she says with a shrug as if to say she didn't care very much. As she looks to Hailey, she couldn't help but still glance at the boy that stood down the hall with his friend.

"Hey," she frowns defensively, "he's not edgy, he's fashionable."
She furrows her brows, not understanding what Kat was trying to say, "what, so he's gay?"
Kat resists the urge to facepalm, "No, nevermind, let's go."
She turns to leave as they were right in front of the doors. Hailey's about to follow her, pouting as she wanted more than anything to talk to the two cute guys she'd saw. But she also longed for food. It was a decision she was too lazy to make in that moment.
"Yah!" a voice was heard behind them, followed by fast footsteps.
Hailey was excited to hear this, but Katarina on the other hand winced, having a feeling as to what was going to happen. Reluctantly, she turned around along with Hailey to face the caramel-haired boy that had jumpily ran up to them, his dark haired friend lazily walking a bit behind.
"Hi, are you two perhaps going to lunch?"

She'd been staring at the screen of her laptop for what felt like hours, and probably was. She was usually quick when it came to things like writing papers, or any sort of work at all. She'd always found herself devoted to schoolwork. 
But right then, she couldn't think of a single word to type into the keyboard before her. Her mind was empty, just like her heart. Her skin was red and tear stained, and her entire body felt numb as she blankly continued to stare at the screen.
When she'd gotten back to her dorm, she'd called Tae. He'd been rather confused to hear from her, as all of the boys had previously been informed she'd been with Yoongi, as he'd answered the phone as cheerily as ever, "Hi, noona, what's up?"
He sounded so happy as he was no doubt with Hails, that it'd hurt her to ruin it. It'd hurt her to tell him. But she had as she'd cleared her throat so he wasn't able to tell how much she'd been sobbing, "I found out everything today, please tell Hailey," she didn't wait for him to reply as the last thing she told him was, "take care of her, don't let her leave."
She knew how this would upset her, too. The thought of her best friend being hurt was something she couldn't bare, especially with everything else happening with her. She didn't want her to feel how she did now.
The reason she had left Yoongi there was for him and the boys. She knew it would be dangerous for them to stay together (or be together in the first place since they hadn't been official.) She didn't want to be an endangerment to their career, their dream. She didn't want to be in a relationship she was unable to be true to due to the fact it would have to only be kept secret for god knows how long.
Taehyung and Hailey were a different story. Yes, it was dangerous, no doubt. But Hailey was part of his dream, the way Taehyung looked at her told it all. He loved her.
She knew Yoongi. He wanted to be known. He wanted to produce and make music. He wasn't like them.
With tears falling from her eyes just like they had been for hours now, she rises from her desk. Grabbing the same bag she'd carried with her ever since she'd came to this college, she digs through it to pull out her journal. It'd felt like a century to her since she'd wrote since she'd visited her parents and been with Yoongi. With all the emotion she felt then, she had a lot to pour out.
So with a shaky sigh, she falls back onto her bed, pen in hand, flipping through the pages to find the first empty one. As she does so, her eyes land on the familiar title at the top of one of the many pages. 
Just One Day
She stares at it for a while, trying to blink away the extra tears that wanted to come out. She couldn't help but glance down at the lyrics, reading over each and every individual word that she'd wrote. She stared even longer at Yoongi's scribbles from the stuff he'd wrote and added. She frowned as she looked down at the journal in her hands. To think that music could bring her so much joy, but so much pain at the same time.
After all, it was the entire reason this was happening to her.
Eventually, she forced herself to turn the page, clicking her pen as she immediately began to write. 
This is where she'd be for god knew how long. Here, writing music, for she had so many things to say and feelings to get out. It was the only way she knew she would ever get over this. Because this was a type of hurt she'd never felt before, emptiness, loss.
It was time for her to go back to her old life. Only focusing on school and getting her degree. That was what needed to be important. But she'd still write music on the side, too. This was something she'd always done, anyway.
As she wrote everything she was feeling onto the paper before her, she couldn't help but let the tears fall along with the words. When they would wet the paper as she wrote, she would just write beside it. The tears would show the her in the future when she read this, or anyone else for that matter, how meaningful it really is.
On top of this ending tune
I am standing here alone
Now tell me that it's over, let me know
Suddenly, in my eyes
Rain wells up
You well up
I see you even when I breathe
Love blooms
Like cherry blossoms

She sets the pen down to harshly bite her lip, trying to stop herself from breaking into sobs. She was in a rather small dorm, and was well aware she had neighbors. What would they think if they heard her? She didn't want to be noisy.
So instead she bites her lip to stop any noise, closing her journal with the pen inside and setting it down beside her on the small bed. Pulling her knees to her chest, she wraps her arms around them to bury her face, breaking down completely as all of the reality slapped her in the face.
Why her? She'd never liked someone so much. She'd never connected with someone so much. She'd never had the same interests with someone so deeply. 
It all sucked. It all made her angry. But nonetheless, she felt lost. Not only was she losing Yoongi, but it felt as if she was losing all the boys, too. She couldn't decide. Should she stay in contact with them? Hailey probably was going to. She knew her best friend well enough. Her and Taehyung were going to stay together, no doubt. They found a way through everything, it would barely matter that he was moving away.

A tired sigh leaves her lips as she notices how dark it was getting outside. She rises to her feet to walk to the window, pulling back the curtains to peer outside. Due to the fact she was so high up as her dorm was on one of the top floors, she had a nice view of the sky from her window. The pretty stars in the night light seemed to distract her momentarily.
She stared up at the same stars as her heart ached. If only she knew Yoongi had been doing the exact same thing, staring at the exact same stars from his window, feeling the exact same heartbreak. And wanting nothing more than to hold her in his arms.

열일곱; Though we are putting an end to our relationship
"You're really not going to stay with Yoongi?" Hailey's voice is full of confusion as she has to jog a bit to keep up with the small girl who was walking at an irregularly fast pace down the sidewalk in front of their college.

She rolls her eyes at her rhetorical question, before burying her face in her hands. Yoongi loved her? Was that even possible? She didn't know how she felt about such a word when it was being used towards her. She'd never even thought of such a thing having to do with her.
"You love him, too, don't you?" she asked when Katarina didn't say anything after a while.
But the small girl just sat there, seemingly in some sort of trance. She was in deep thought, and her best friend's question only made her think more. Did she love Yoongi? It was such a heavy weight question. She was scared to answer it, she was scared to know the answer.
She had been trying so hard to think of the future, of the boys future. And for them, she knew she couldn't answer it honestly.

This causes her eyes to widen as she watches the small girl then rise to her feet quickly. She grabs the bag that she'd set beside her and hurriedly throws it over her shoulder. Hailey could only sit there in surprise and confusion as she watched the girl that had been before her walk away. Her hair blew in the wind, and she didn't look back at her once.

열아홉; I will get to meet you again
Hoseok frantically pushed passed the crowds of drunk bodies that were either dancing or having some sort of heated makeout session. His eyes darted over every single human in each room as he went through them, in search for one girl and one girl only.
Usually, he and his friends would casually attend these parties. They used to practically every week (except for the third week of each month,) even though all of them except for the girls weren't even in college anymore. The parties were always good ones, and there was nothing more fun than getting drunk with your friends and just letting go, relieving any stress you'd previously had on your shoulders.
This was clearly the thought process he assumed Kat was having. That, and she wanted to forget about it all period. Over the course of him knowing her, she was never one who liked to drink nor get high. Katarina was the type who just tagged along with her friends but never did anything more than that. She would just sit down awkwardly and watch as they all had fun whilst sitting on her phone, most likely working on an English assignment through the Google Docs app.
It was no lie she was a bit of a complete nerd. But it was something Hobi saw as a good quality about her.
He didn't know why, but as soon as he'd heard the news about what was happening when Hailey had gotten back, he had to come as soon as possible. There'd been something different forming inside him towards his old friend, something he was unsure about and couldn't seem to form the words to explain. He just wanted to make sure she was okay, he felt the need to.
His breath was growing ragged from him practically running all over the entire sorority house, which was really fucking large. There were so many people here that he'd never even seen before, how was he supposed to find her?
He'd never been so worried before. The others probably weren't even here yet as Hailey had been having a hard time with Yoongi. He didn't know what it was with that boy. He was so naive when it came to something as simple as just being in a relationship. How could someone be so witty but yet so dumb?
He continued to search for what felt like forever. But as he pushed past more and more people he only felt more and more hopeless.
Soon, he'd reached the kitchen, which most people weren't allowed in. Luckily, he was a friend of Sungyeol, so the guy that guarded it recognized him with just a nod. Hobi sent him one of his signature smiles as he entered.
He let out a deep sigh of relief at the fact he wasn't stuck in the crowds anymore. Clearly, this didn't change the fact he was still worried. And as he looked up, the thought that she might be in here crossing his mind, he was only let down.
However, his eyes were met with the sight of someone else he knew rather well.
"Hoseok! How are you?!" Sungyeol's walking over, a beer in hand, to give him a quick one-armed hug.
Hoseok returned the friendly gesture, trying his best to put on a smile that said I'm perfectly fine. Which was actually something he tended to be good at. As much as he'd like to sit and have a drink with his old friend, he knew there was no time for something as silly as that.
So, instead, he didn't bother to answer his question. Instead, he hurriedly asked, "Have you seen Katarina?"
Sungyeol's expression grew to show one of confusion as he read the worry in his friend's voice. He paused in thought for a moment, thinking hard on where he'd seen the short girl. Hoseok waited, nervously fiddling with his hands as he did so.
"I think I saw her go outside just a while ago," he finally concludes with a big grin.
Hoseok's eyes widen in excitement as he immediately pushes past Sungyeol, who had turned around. He'd heard his friend offer him a beer, but it was too late for him to answer as he was already pushing through the crowds to reach the door that led into the large back yard.
After getting passed all the drunk late-teens and early-twenty year olds, he reached the huge sliding doors. Rushing outside, the cold air hit his skin, clinging onto him for life and instantly sending chills up his spine. He hadn't paid attention to the weather enough to think it would've been wise to wear a jacket tonight.
The wind blew through his hair, brushing it in his face as he began to walk across the yard. He brushed it away as the scent of weed filled his nostrils. He wasn't surprised at this, as the backyard was where people usually smoked.
Continuing his search, he looked desperately everywhere he could think. His feet padded through the tall, green grass as he peered around one of the corners, feeling empty and lost. Where could she possibly be?
Everywhere he looked he grew hopeful, just to be let down all over again.
He sighed helplessly as he walked to the last corner that was on the left side of the house, which was also the darkest as the moon was on the opposite side tonight. He had a feeling he might end up running into people making out or more, which would definitely disturb him for a while. But there was also that small percentage of a chance that Kat was back there, and he held onto that as he grew closer.
Just as he reached it, his ears picked up the sound of someone breathing rather frantically. As the wind blew heavier and heavier, the worst thought filled his head. He prayed to the gods that that wasn't what he was about to witness as he dared himself to turn the corner.
That was when he heard it. Brief, quiet sobs, that ended in some sort of high-pitched squeak. He only knew one person who cried like that.
He didn't waste any time to turn the corner.
What he witnessed tore his heart a bit.
Nothing had felt worse than seeing one of his closest friends curled up in a ball in the dark, her knees pulled up to her chest where her face was buried. She was breathing heavy and rapidly as she sobbed, coughing every once in a while. Hobi didn't know if she was drunk, but he did know one thing.
All of them knew well that Kat had anxiety. She'd told them the story of how she used to have huge problems with it as a child, but as she grew older it was less apparent. I only have it every now in then. Like if something really bad happens, or if I'm by myself and don't feel well. She'd said, and as he saw her trembling body, he knew that was exactly what was happening.
His feet were quick as he rushed to her aid. He slowly lifted her up, her name leaving his lips in a soft manner.
"Kat? Kat, it's okay," he tried to tell her, unaware if she was even listening as she only continued to cry.
Her eyes were still slammed shut as he slowly pulled her into his arms. He hugged her tightly, whispering in her ear every few seconds as an attempt to calm her down. He'd never seen her have an attack before, and he realized that now that he had, he never wanted her to have one again.
"Sh, it's okay," he kept saying, trying to get her to snap out of the 'trance' she seemed to be stuck in.
"I'm sorry," he hears her finally speak through her tears. He didn't know who she was trying to apologize to, and he didn't question it further as he just held her there. Her voice came out weak and broken, so much that she could barely speak those two words.
It was clear she'd drank a bit. And all the people plus the slight intoxication had caused her body to shut down.
"It's okay," Hobi tried to reassure her repeatedly as she kept mumbling the two words over and over.
Moments and moments passed, and he continued to just hold her there. Leaning back against the wall, he released one arm from around her to pull out his phone, making sure to send a quick text to his friends to make sure they knew he'd found her.
Suddenly, she began to move a bit, and the sobbing sounds had began to stop. This had caused him to set his phone aside despite the fact it was beginning to ding rapidly with texts from his friends wanting to know what was going on and where they were.
She slowly lifted her head, her eyes barely open but just enough so she could see where she was and who was holding her. Hobi shifted a bit at the sight of her waking up, not saying anything as her red, green eyes slowly met his.
"H-Hobi?" she made out his name, sounding confused at first. Practically a thousand emotions spread over her face in that moment, before a look of relief appeared.
He could barely process what was happening before she rushed to hug him, still being in his lap. Kat was just glad she wasn't alone anymore.
However her action had greatly confused him a bit, but he slowly hugged her back as she wrapped her arms around him firmly. Katarina didn't even have memories of the last few hours, she had just wanted to forget - to forget everything.
But she should've known better. She hadn't done anything like drinking in a long time, not to mention she'd went to do it by herself. All the people had ended up being too much for her. All the thoughts poking at her brain, all the mistakes.
"Thank you," she whispers, her voice still not back to normal as it was barely audible.
But Hobi had heard her clearly as he only smiled, just glad she was okay, "I was worried about you." He says as she pulls away from the hug to just sit there, looking at him.
Katarina sniffles as she runs a hand through her hair. Her breathing still wasn't completely back to normal due to the anxiety attack she'd just had, but it was getting there. Slowly, she glanced down at what she was wearing, before looking back up at Hobi and chuckling dryly, "I dressed nice and everything."
He lightly laughed as he looked at her. A million thoughts pressed through his brain in that moment, but the main one was that he wanted to make her feel better. So he threw on his signature sunshine grin, "you look beautiful."
The sudden compliment had taken her aback as she met his eyes again. There was a look in them she didn't have the energy to read, nor did she feel like pressing into the matter anymore period. So she just nervously looked to the ground, "thanks."
Hoseok figured it would be a good idea to update her on where everyone was, especially Yoongi. But part of him just wanted to be there with her in that moment. It was the only time he'd really gotten alone with her other than that moment in the bathroom.
He knew a part of her was probably wondering, though.
With this, he opens his mouth to speak, but before he could, the sound of hectic voices and fast footsteps are heard from where Hobi had previously come from. The two's heads jerk up towards the commotion that was coming right for them.
The sight of their friends caused their eyes to widen, as they hadn't expected them to find them any time soon.
"Kat, oh my fucking god," Hailey yelled so loud some of them felt the urge to cover their ears, but didn't because the moment was too important as the pink haired girl rushed towards her best friend. She fell on her knees to hug Katarina, who was awkwardly still in Hobi's lap.
"hi," Kat only mumbled as he hugged her best friend back.
The others walked to be beside her also as Hailey sent her that knowing look of hers, "you're an idiot."
"Please don't ever do that again," Jin was saying as a frown was evident on his face. He was just like the worried mother they all saw him as.
"I'm sorry," she sent him an apologetic smile, but he shook his head.
"Don't apologize, I'm glad you're okay," he sent her one of his 'worldwide handsome smiles,' before the others said their reliefs to her, too.
The air grew quiet, as everyone was just sort of sitting there for a moment. To be honest, they were all taking in the fact that everything was almost okay. But there was one large thing left to fix.
The thought pinged in Katarina's head as she looked around at all of her friends, her eyesight a bit blurry from the previous events. Where was Yoongi? her brain thought frantically. More than anything, she missed him. She missed him so bad.
She'd hated lying to Hailey that day. She'd hated telling him they couldn't be together. She'd hated trying to convince herself that she wasn't selfish. She'd hated spending late nights alone, all by herself, writing sad song lyrics.
If anything, she just wanted to see him. She just wanted to see his dark, straight locks that almost covered his eyes and look into his deep, chocolate orbs. She just wanted to hear his voice. That was all she wanted, before she decided anything else.

She saw him.
Upon the sight of the boy, she felt herself almost have an attack all over again. Her eyes widened a bit, and her friends noticed as they looked at her in confusion, before looking towards what she was so surprised by.

She was rather taken aback to say the least. His hair was fucking red. Yoongi had talked about wanting to try dyeing his hair, and she'd always shrugged when he would ask her what color should be first.
How about mint green? Ooh, or maybe just flat out platinum?
He'd never seemed to like any of her suggestions. And now here he was, having had done it, with red hair.
He'd never looked so good.
He slowly approached the group, his eyes raking over everyone but her. It wasn't long before they did fall on her, and then went to Hobi. His brows furrowed at the sight of her on his lap, which she realized she hadn't moved from.
This caused her eyes to bulge a bit as she hurriedly rushed to sit onto the grass instead, not wanting him to get the wrong idea.

She felt rather awkward in that moment. A part of her wanted to run to him, but she didn't feel like that would be the best idea. As far as he knew, she'd told him they couldn't be together. And even then, she didn't know if she'd changed her mind or not.
It was true, he had still wanted to be with her despite the rule. He said he didn't care for it, he didn't want it to exist. So why did she?
Yoongi didn't say anything to Hailey's remark. He just slowly stopped before the friends that were all sitting on the grass. As he stood there, he seemed to be in very deep thought. It was clear he didn't know what to do either.
His eyes didn't meet hers as she looked up at him from her seat on the ground. Feeling shy since he wasn't even looking back, she instead directed to eyes to the ground, biting her lip nervously as she tried to think.
Hobi glanced to the girl that sat beside him before looking back to Yoongi. He wasn't sure what the two were thinking then, but he could tell neither of them had any idea what they should say or do.
Katarina was just fiddling with her fingers in her lap when Hobi's voice broke the silence, "Maybe it's not the best for you to be here, Yoongi." His words surprised everyone and even Hobi himself as all eyes fell on him.

"I think I'm going to stay at my parents."
The sudden, confident statement her best friend had just spoken out of nowhere caused Katarina's once relaxed body to tense. Hailey laid her head on the small girl's shoulder, letting out a shaky sigh as she sniffled, trying to make the tears that kept managing to escape her eyes leave. Her parents were always very supportive of her, they would understand, right? Her mother had had her when she was young, also. There was no way they could get upset with her.
But something that rushed into her worries was college. Although, yes, she didn't show much care at all for her silly education that she was tired of going through all her life, she did need to do something about it if she wasn't even going to be living near it anymore. She had to drop out.

Once this was done she'd turned her back against the counter to lean back on it, a yawn leaving her lips. Her green irises stared at everything from the walls to the dining table, and she reminisced about those easy times. Sleeping being one of his few hobbies and things that he enjoyed to consume his time with, he was for sure dreaming about her.
Yoongi was so enveloped in his sweet slumber that he had no idea of the events that were happening around him in the van. Thus being Hoseok wildly laughing as he snapped multiple photos of Yoongi's derp-y sleeping expression, Taehyung laughing with him and at Jungkook's pain due to the fact Yoongi had been pushed limplessly onto the maknae's lap, all with Jimin telling them their actions probably weren't very smart. Not to mention, Namjoon and Jin who were sitting so close together in the front seats that they looked glued to each other as some old 90s song of Jin's choice played from the radio.
This was a typical car ride with the seven boys.
"We're on the street!" the voice of Taehyung was heard as he squealed that of a child in pure excitement. Being by the window in the back row, he'd put his hands on the tinted window, pressing his face against the glass to see everything on the familiar street clearly. The unbeatable rush was practically choking him as they passed each and every house he used to see every morning on the way to college, and it only made him more eager to see the girl he loved.
"Thanks for the info, Taehyung, I would've never guessed," Hoseok hadn't waited to make his sarcastic remark to the obviously excited boy. He knew how happy he was, and hell, Hoseok was, too. But everyone knew how he loved to make jokes, he could never help himself.
Either way, the comment had caused the puppy-like boy sitting in the back seat beside the not so fortunate Jungkook and sleeping Yoongi to frown in annoyance at his friend, who was seated directly in front of him. Hoseok had caught his expression and laughed, "Joking, I know you're excited."
As they continued the drive down the road, the commotion in the vehicle had rose with each passing millisecond. Everyone was practically yelling at the top of their lungs at this point, and as Jungkook looked down at his lap where the sleeping boy was, he couldn't help but think to himself how the actual fuck the boy wasn't awake yet. If he's so excited to see noona, how the fuck could he even fall asleep in the first place?
"Aish," he mumbled to himself, directing his brown eyes to instead look out the window, "I'll never understand Yoongi-hyung."
The poor maknae continued to watch the familiar scenery he missed pass outside, his ears being filled with the excited squeals of Taehyung. The others were obviously all excited too, (he's sure Jimin was having a hard time hiding it, he was probably exactly like Taehyung inside.) But they weren't going bat-shit crazy like their child like friend. He guessed he couldn't blame him since he was so excited to see the girl he loved, and Jungkook felt bad at the recent fact he'd found out about: Hailey wasn't going to even be there.
It was something he knew would break not only Taehyung's, but probably Jimin's heart, too. He wished he could tell them she wasn't there, but it would only lead them to ask the question he didn't even know the answer to yet: just why did she go back to Busan?
"Arrived," the Google maps woman had instructed, causing the 90s song that had been playing to be turned down so that everyone could hear her clearly. The thing was, the volume had been turned up so loud that the sound of the booming, robot-like voice scared them a bit, before they'd all looked out the window to see just exactly they'd arrived at much like it had instructed: home.
"We're home," the eldest had called back the obvious to the others as he'd powered off the vehicle they'd been stuck in for so long, "I'd recommend waking Yoongi up now."
The others in the middle and back rows had nodded, paying good attention to their elder's words respectfully. This included everyone except for Taehyung, who was too busy kicking his feet on the back of Hoseok'sseat, screaming at the top of his lungs, "Let me out, let me out!"
Hoseok had been busy gathering his things such as earbuds and electronics, and had tried to ignore the eager boy behind him at first. Jin and Namjoon had already climbed out of the van and made their way to the back to begin collecting the bags, and Taehyung wanted nothing more than to desperately run to the door, break it down, and see his girl. But Hobi was preventing him from doing such, and it was sending him into quite the frenzy.
"Alright, alright, calm your fucking balls!" Hoseok had cried in annoyance, finally getting all of his things and putting his hand on the door handle, forcing it open.
The moment the caramel haired boy had witnessed it open, his eyes getting a clear sight of the outside, he'd bolted like a fucking animal. Taehyung had skyrocketed over the back seat, pushing Hoseok who was just climbing out as he did so, but he didn't care about anything else in that moment that didn't have to do with seeing her.
"Pabo," Hoseok had groaned from the fact he'd been pushed like that, dusting himself off as he watched the boy scramble up the steps to the porch.
Whilst such was happening, everyone else had climbed out of the car to begin to unload their bags. But Jungkook continued to sit in the spot he'd been stuck in for hours, unable to move his legs due to the boy that was sleeping atop them. He knew how much Yoongi hated people waking him up, and he'd tried to let him get his 'beauty sleep' in. Plus, he wouldn't mind since they were seeing noona, right?
So heaving out a sigh, the youngest had reached up his pointer finger, before poking the slumbering bear's cheek a few times.
He didn't move a muscle.
Jungkook frowned at the fact he was sleeping so soundly. Am I that comfortable?! He raised his hands to gently push Yoongi this time, but only grew frustrated when he yet again didn't move an inch, the quiet snores and small breathe's of slumber still pouring from his parted lips.
He hadn't meant his next actions to be as harsh as they were, and he would most likely get killed in his sleep for them later. Raising his hands once again, he'd pushed Yoongi accidentally rather harshly, his annoyance seeming to get the best of him when the previously sleeping boy had fell to the ground of the vehicle.
This had definitely woken Yoongi up, and as his eyes shot open like a hawk, he had no fucking idea what had just happened.
"Yah -- what the actual-," he was in the middle of mumbling tiredly, wanting nothing more than to sleep again and hurt whoever dared to wake him up from such as he weakly rose to sit up, climbing upon the seat again.
But his words had been cut off by the young boy who sat beside him, who Yoongi had no clue he'd fell asleep on all this time, "You slept the entire time, look outside, hyung."
Not obeying the maknae's actions at first, Yoongi furrowed his brows in confusion as everything that was reality began to slowly flow back into his head. His conscience returned as he was persuading from hearing the commotion of his friend's voices outside as they were carrying the bags to the porch of a certain house.
His eyes widened as he let them trail to look out the opened door in the row in front of them, they were here.
"Holy shit," he'd mumbled, rising to his feet instantly and climbing over the seat. Yoongi had heard Jungkook chuckle at his sudden realization of the fact they were home after all this time, but he didn't care to turn and make a witty comment like he would any other day.
He had to see her.

"Sorry not sorry I couldn't come to the phone right now, I'm probably busy-" Hailey's giggly tone was heard over the recording Kat had been listening to over and over for what felt like years now. Every time she got cut off by an excited Taehyung screaming in the background.
"She's busy with me!" he'd yell before there's shuffling on the line, and then the sound of her laughs fill your ears.
It'd end off every time with her squealing, "so anyway, I'll call you back -- or probably not, bye!"
Katarina had removed the phone from her ear to end the call once again, before pressing the green 'call back' button. This was a routine she'd done for the last twenty minutes, trying to get a hold of her best friend who hadn't spoken to her since their last phone call where she'd insisted for Kat not to worry about her. Ever since then, she hadn't replied or even read any of her texts nor returned her calls.
She said not to worry about her, but how the fuck am I supposed to not when she won't even reply to me?! She hated not being able to be there for her best friend, but maybe she was just -- busy?
But hell, one text back would be nice.

She'd removed the phone from her ear this time to hear furious knocking coming from the front door.

But she cared too much for not only her dear friend's, but her best friend, Hailey's, being to do such a thing. She had to let Hailey tell him everything herself, for their twisted road of a relationship wasn't her's to walk down.

He expected them to have a cute reunion full of tight hugs and a trillion kisses. Taehyung expecting anything other than the fact she didn't appear, and the expression that was found on his noona's face once he had looked back down to her.
It gave him an uneasy feeling. Obviously, he wasn't an idiot, and this was all to weird for him to not grow suspicious. But he didn't want to think that the worst thing that could've been, had actually happened.
"What's wrong, noona?" he'd furrowed his brows, refusing to believe any bad thoughts in his head. Perhaps she was upstairs sleeping, but why did Katarina look so distressed?
Her green irises were full of sympathy when they looked up to him again. The dark haired girl had shook her head, strands of hair falling in her face as she did so. "Just come inside, Tae," she'd hummed to him, stepping aside the doorway she'd been standing in to allow him to enter.

Despite this, it was a kiss that was full of more meaning than the human brain could even begin to comprehend, it was a kiss that made everything in her world okay again.

"Taehyung, sit down," Kat had said shakily, and the boy hadn't even met her eyes as he did so.

It was something she was glad he was providing her, being the rather jealous but still perfect boyfriend she'd always wanted. It wasn't that this news was hard to break to them, she just didn't want Jimin and Taehyung to be upset.
"So, Hails uh -- she's not here because she had to go back to Busan," she'd cleared her throat before explaining the story her and Hailey had decided to go with, "the reason being she had some er -- family issues, that were really urgent. She had to go back ASAP and miss my birthday and seeing you guys," she'd went on, trying not to wince from the lie (although it wasn't really a complete one,) "she's having a hard time, so please understand why she hasn't been replying."
She's not fucking replying to me, either, she wanted to bitterly add but didn't. Hails probably was just caught up with something, and she wasn't going to get freaked out about it despite the fact she couldn't help but be slightly worried and confused.
Her eyes had raked over everyone's expression when she'd finally broke the news. Everyone obviously wasn't happy at the unfortunate news, especially Taehyung who's frown practically reached his chin. His head hung down as he seemed to be thinking or crying, and she felt awful for the emotions he was probably feeling.
The next person she noticed was Jimin. Jimin wasn't trying to show how sad he was, but she could see he was hurt about the news also as he directed his eyes to his feet.
She only sighed, shaking her head before turning and burying her face into Yoongi's chest. This ended up surprising him a bit, but assuming she was probably feeling a bit uneasy right then, he hadn't waited to wrap his arm around her shoulder, allowing her to comfortably hide like a child.
The silence in the room seemed to make not only Taehyung, and not only Katarina, but everyone think. It caused them all to think rather hard about the events that were going on. Yoongi's mind was stuck on his girlfriend's surprise party that he needed to go prepare, and how that disgusting bitch might actually show up there, as he had to invite her for the sake of his career. Katarina's mind was on the exam she had to take that night, and the unfortunate fact her ex boyfriend was the one giving her said exam. Namjoon was thinking about the choreographer he'd invited to the party like an idiot, risking the fact that she could realize Katarina and Yoongi were breaking the contract. Jimin and Taehyung were both helplessly stuck on how badly they missed Hailey and wanted to speak to her, to make sure she was okay. Neither of them had heard her voice in so long, and it was a drug they badly missed taking. And lastly, Jin was worrying about what they were going to eat -- which was the least of everyone else's worries but the top of his.

오십; My birth and the end of my life
It was 5 PM when Yoongi had finally managed to get everyone to leave the two of them alone. He'd been wanting to spend time with her for so long, but when he had finally gotten the chance Jungkook, Hoseok, and especially Taehyung had kept barging in the room. Not to mention, they always wanted something completely fucking stupid. It had him completely prepared to slaughter all three of them at the same time as he'd pushed Taehyung out of his bedroom one last time, telling him sternly, "don't fucking come back if you want to keep your legs," to which he'd slammed the door in the caramel boys face, before locking it.
He'd turned back to his girlfriend who was lounging on his bed, laying on her side and keeping her head up with her arm. Expecting her to be laughing at his usual negative comment meant towards their friend, she was instead frowning as he'd went to sit back beside her.
There was nothing he hated more than seeing the girl he loved so down. Reaching up a finger, he poked her cheek with his index finger, causing the previously frowning girl to wrinkle her nose as he did so. "yah!" she'd mumbled, swatting his finger away with her small hand as he'd chuckled at her.
"What's wrong?" he hadn't waited to question her in concern. Laying on his back, his body seemed to sink into the comfortable mattress he'd missed so badly. The girl beside him hadn't done the same, and only continued to stare down at him, her expression remaining blank.
Unhappy with her actions, he'd grabbed her arm that had been holding her body up, forcing her to lay down -- directly on top of him. She'd squealed in laughter as he did so, surprised at his sudden straight forward actions.
"hey, chill out!" she complained as he held her wrists with both of his hands so she couldn't get off of him, forcing her to meet his dark brown orbs.
"I'll chill out when you tell me what you're so down about."
Katarina let out a dull sigh at this. It wasn't a sigh that meant she didn't want to tell him, she just didn't know if she really felt like talking about it anymore. But at the same time, she just couldn't help but feel bad.
"I feel bad for Tae and Chim," she'd explained, voicing her worries, "do you think I should've told them she wasn't here earlier? I feel like I ruined their entire trip," her green eyes filled with sadness as they met her boyfriend's.
His heart seemed to shatter in his chest, just the sight of her like this. Yoongi was quick to shake his head at her, sitting the two of them up. She was surprised as he did so, and this ended up with her in his lap, but she didn't care much like she did previously.
"Stop worrying about them, it's not your problem," he'd let go of her wrists at this point, and they were sitting by her side as her legs were wrapped around his waist. Yoongi had picked up one of her hands to kiss the back of it repeatedly as a calming action as he reassured her, "you didn't ruin anything, it's Hailey's love life to deal with, focus on yours."
She pouted at his words, knowing Yoongi was right. He was always fucking right, it was something she hated but loved about him.
So she'd tried to push the thoughts to the very back of her head, thinking back to the last words he had said to her. "Well, mine is right in front of me," she'd joked, giggling a bit as she said such a cringeworthy comment.
Yoongi had for sure noticed how cringe it was as he'd wrinkled his nose, "you're lucky you're cute, jagiya."
"I know," she'd nodded matter-of-factly, "and you love me."
Her boyfriend wasn't phased to admit like he was all those months ago, "of course I do," he hummed casually, his eyes trailing around his own bedroom and disconnecting from her green ones for a moment. He was in search of something in particular, and he soon found it when he saw that certain piano sitting against the wall in the far corner of his darkly painted room. Her journal sat atop of it, pencil shoved in between some of the pages which let him know she had been writing recently.
It only rose questions he was eager to know the answers to, "what have you been working on?" his eyes had looked to her immediately after he'd saw her journal. It was such a sudden movement she'd jumped a bit, having had been distracted by playing with his hair that she noticed was a lot lighter. The stylists must of bleached it a bit before he left, she couldn't help but wonder what color it was going to be for the boys comeback as the red velvet was now a orange-ish color instead.
He hadn't cared much for his girlfriend messing with his hair due to how badly he wanted an answer to his question. Kat had been in the middle of braiding a small braid with his bangs when she'd finally looked to him, "uh, nothing very much."
Yoongi pouted at the response as she'd been distracted by his hair soon once again. He'd reached up to grab her hand that was messing with his hair, "jagi~, show me what you were working on."
She knew she had told herself earlier she was going to show him the song. But she knew he meant playing it on the piano too, and she didn't trust her piano skills. Not yet, she hadn't gotten to practice as much as she would've wanted over those months, and she didn't think she was up to par with him yet. When she finally played for him, she wanted it to be impressive, and then definitely was not the time.
Which was why she winced a bit, trying to look away from his adorable pleading gaze but it pended to be rather impossible. Yah, why does he have to be so irresistible?
"But Yoongi-" she couldn't get anymore than those two words out before he'd cut her off.
"Please~, you promised me."
Knowing there was no way she could get out of this, she groaned in defeat, making her way off her lap. "Fine," her voice was a mumble as her bare feet hit the soft carpet, and she made her way to the portable keyboard piano that sat in the corner of Yoongi's room.
He was right behind her as she sat down, and he'd sat right beside her, curiously peeking as her small hands handled her journal. She's so careful with everything she does, he watched her fingers slowly flip through each page admiringly. It wasn't long until she'd stopped at a certain page. Upon it were about a verse of lyrics, along with piano notes written above each part. It impressed him how much she'd seemed to teach herself on her own, and her passion only seemed to warm his heart for her more.
"Okay, it's gonna be really bad, please don't judge me," she'd told him worriedly with pleading eyes.
Yoongi shook his head disapprovingly at her, "just play, I won't believe you until I hear you myself."
Heaving out a shaky sigh, he'd only shot her that deadly grin as she'd placed her hands over the correct keys. Closing her eyes for a split second, she looked up at the journal she had set on the stand atop the piano, telling herself she had nothing to worry about. It's just Yoongi.
And then she began after clearing her throat, letting the words she'd wrote from her heart pour from her throat and her fingers dance across the keys. It took all of her thought process, so much that she had no time to even glance at her boyfriend to see his reaction as she did so. All she could hope for was that it wasn't a bad one.
Will you stay by my side?
Will you promise me?
If I let go of your hand, you'll fly away and break.
I'm scared, I'm scared of that.
Will you stop time?
If this moment passes
As though it hadn't happened
I'm scared, scared I'll lose you
Just when she thought she was doing well, she messed up on the part she always fucking messed up on. She'd only managed to play it correctly once just barely, and ever since then she couldn't seem to get it right.
Cursing at herself in frustration, she was about to slam her hands on the piano out of annoyance with herself and the fact she always tended to mess up at the same part. Just as she was raising her hands to do so, she felt two larger, stronger hands being placed over hers, gently guiding her hands to certain keys.
Startled at first, she didn't move a muscle as her boyfriend had placed her fingers over the notes she had been attempting to play correctly only moments ago. All she knew to do was stay still and watch as he pressed down on her fingers, going slower than it was supposed to be since he was guiding her. Surely but slowly, he'd begun to play the melody she had been working so hard on correctly.
Once the portion of the melody that she had been struggling with ended, his hands had slowly removed themselves from atop hers. "It's like that," he'd informed, "you already play so well, I'm so proud of you, jagi~."
Her cheeks had turned pink from his compliments she wasn't used to receiving in person still, and to hide it she'd focused on the journal that still sat in front of her. There was a moment of silence as her eyes skimmed over the words she'd wrote with him in mind, each one had poured from her heart so effortlessly.
Yoongi had noticed her staring at the song, and reached out a hand to point at the part she'd played wrong previously, "Here, try playing it again," he'd instructed like he was some sort of teacher.
His instruction was definitely not one she wanted to follow as she'd looked at him in annoyance. "Why, can't you play me something? It's your turn."
He'd wrinkled his nose jokingly, but shrugged anyway, not minding her suggestion, "Alright, if you insist." She'd let out a breathe of relief at the fact he had let his previous request go, scooting over so he could be perfectly in the middle.
Just before he'd begun playing he'd looked at her with that lopsided joking smile of his, "be prepared, you're about to witness genius."
"yah, just play!"
He'd exploded with laughter as her harsh comment, but had obeyed as his fingers had begun to dance perfectly across the keys. All she could do was watch in awe, her eyes glancing repeatedly from his focused expression that managed to somehow make him more beautiful to his hands that swayed across the instrument he'd seemed to be indeed a master at. Passion poured from the words he began to rap, each one warming her heart and only making her love him more with admiration. This boy was her everything, it was a fact she knew for sure.
Laying her head on his shoulder, she continued to listen to the peaceful melody he played and the way his voice seemed to combine with it. In that moment, not only Katarina, but Yoongi too had forgotten everything. All of their worries seemed to fly right out the window of the house that it had all started in. They knew, they knew they'd be okay despite everything that they worried would happen. As long as we have each other, we're unbreakable, right?
Yoongi would make sure it was something that would be true. He wouldn't let Samantha ruin the party he still had planned, he was going to make it the most amazing birthday she could ever ask for. He would make sure that vile bitch didn't have the proof to ruin his relationship and career anymore -- at least he hoped he would find a way.
And Katarina didn't care about the stupid exam she had to take that she knew she aced already the first time. She would finish it with ease, make sure her horrid ex boyfriend grading it deservingly this time, and she'd come right back home to him and celebrate her birthday with her best friends and the love of her life.
Nothing can get in their way.

The last thing he wanted to do was rightfully admit he really did or used to have feelings for his girlfriend, because that would only end in for sure blood and bruises.
A few people were staring at him as he scurried away from the flaming boy, having had overheard the heated conversation. Hoseok kept his head down as he pushed through the crowds, wanting nothing more than to forget about what had happened.
He felt rather worried now. Yoongi might actually kill him when he found out what his present to Kat was. He thought HE would be performing... Yoongi was really in for a surprise.
A dull sigh had left his lips, because despite it all, the last thing Hoseok had wanted was to get in a fight with Yoongi. It would only make everything awkward between them, especially at work. What the hell was he supposed to do?
Wanting nothing more than to just go sit down from everything he'd been up to back stage, he decided to make his way towards the sofa where everyone in the friend group would be sitting at. His feet were quick under him as he continued pushing through all the people, a few greeting him since they were college friends, but he was too bothered to even reply.
What had knocked him back into reality was the sudden feeling of someone running into him -- or more like him running into them. He felt someone that was for sure shorter than him face-palm into his chest, and he'd snapped out of his thoughts to hurriedly step back from whoever he'd ran into.
Not paying the girl much attention at first, he'd began with a, "Shit, I'm really sorry, I wasn't watching where I was going-," but he cut himself off once he saw just exactly who he had ran into in the first place.
It was definitely not someone he would of expected.
"Jesus, this is the second time," Xzoriah had giggled, her tone not at all as toxic as it usually was towards the boy. She wasn't really surprised he, and most likely the other Bangtan Boys, where here. In all honesty, she was just glad she had finally found someone she knew, even if it was her 'dance rival.'
Hoseok seemed awestruck as he'd stared down at her, trying to piece together any pieces in his head whatsoever. How was she here? Who invited her? What if she finds out we're breaking the contract? There were a trillion questions flying around his head frantically, and he was at a complete loss for words.
The choreographer seemed to notice this as she stared at the sunshine boy, her brows furrowing from how he seemed to be lost in some sort of trance.
"Ho-Ho, you good?" She'd asked, waving a hand in front of his face to try to get him to come back to Earth from whatever dimension he'd disappeared to.
He seemed to come back only because of the stupid name she had called him that he hated with a strong passion. "I'm great, how are you even here?" he had instead gotten right to the point, his voice coming out rather demanding. He was just trying to understand, had Namjoon invited her? Surely their leader wouldn't do such a thing, he was smarter than that. Hoseok didn't know her very well, but there was no way they could trust her with knowing the fact they were breaking the contract.
Xzoriah was rather taken aback from his sudden harsh tone directed at no one other than herself. Her expression came one of defensiveness as she crossed her arms over her chest, "Yah, don't have to be so rude, I get that I look out of place or whatever," she'd snapped, "Namjoon invited me, thank you very much."
So Namjoon had invited her, his brain confirmed. It was almost hard for him to believe. Did he not think of how dangerous her being at Kat's party was?!
He didn't know what else to say to her, so she only shook his head, "Just don't ruin anything."
This was all he was going to say as his feet had already begun walking away. But Hobi had only taken one step when he felt a small hand grab his arm, pulling him right back to where he'd been seconds ago. For such a small girl, she sure had a fucking grip.

Truthfully she didn't expect Hoseok to tell her shit, she was just really confused and eager to find out anything at all.
She knew well enough of that so she wasn't very surprised when Hoseok had shook his head, "you'll see soon enough anyway," before he'd left without another word.

15 minutes ago
baby kookie: kat, yoongi-hyung said you won't answer his texts. are u ok?

He knew easily he could be lying, cause what kind of coincidence is that? She most likely hadn't thought of it as a big deal being as she didn't know about the party.

This guy has some serious mental issues, he shook his head, his blood boiling from his rather fucked up words.

Katarina sped up her pace to a jog as she rushed towards the two boys. One she knew for sure was her professor and ex boyfriend, but she was unsure as to who the second one was. Fuck, he probably got worried about me, and now Jungkook knows. She mentally cursed at her idiotic self, but rushed towards the maknae anyway.

Pulling away from his grip on her hand, she turned to Monty, "I don't know why you tried to hurt him, but I wouldn't recommend doing it again," she snapped sternly as if she was the eldest out of the two. Everything seemed to be on track again -- for everyone but Yoongi,at least that's what it felt like. meanwhile, when Jungkook and Katarina had arrived to the club, she was rather confused. She wasn't the brightest when it came to the assumption that people might be doing something for her, so she couldn't seem to piece together why they were at one of the most popular nightclub's in Daejeon.

How was Hails, who still hadn't replied to her or called yet? Katarina was completely clueless to the fact that all the cars piled in to the parking lot belonged to people she knew.

Her hands were shaking at her sides as she stared at the girl in slight fear and confusion, "who are you?"
Samantha couldn't help but snort a bit at the girl's shaking voice. What the hell is with his taste in girls? This girl is like a fucking child. "I'm your boyfriend's stylist, sweetheart, and I snagged this from his bag after hearing him and his friends talk a bit too much about a particular girl," the smirk was inevitably washed onto her face at that point, "If you're unaware, I'll be glad to tell you your 'boyfriend' isn't allowed to date as long as he's under the contract of Big Hit Studios, who my father is head producer of," Katarina's eyes were practically on the floor from having fell out of their sockets from disbelief. This isn't really happening, someone tell me this isn't real. She shakily pinched her arm, her brain screaming to wake up, but she never did. This was really happening.

But the mystery girl didn't seem to care in the slightest about whatever she was attempting, "break up with Yoongi, or the entirety of Bangtan Sonyeondan's career will be over, and it'll all be thanks to you."

The pink haired girl's hands were shaky as she walked, along with her entire body. She'd tried to dress nice for the special occasion, but she didn't have a good range of fancy maternity clothes, so she'd ended up showing up rather casually.

She had decided to enter through the very back, where the back stage would be located at. This was because she wanted no attention on her whatsoever. This was Kat and Yoongi's night, and she didn't want to ruin it with her problems. All the wanted was to talk to two boys in particular.

meet me backstage asap

They both of them, however, had stopped dead in their tracks at the sight of the thirteen boys they'd witnessed standing there together. Taehyung knew immediately who they were, as his eyes widened and he screamed with surprise, "What, Yoongi-hyung actually got her favorite group to perform?!"
The boys of Seventeen had all been laughing about something, seeming to have been making jokes and messing around with each other. At the sound of Tae's voice, they'd all turned in unison.
At the realization all of their eyes were on him now from his loudness, Taehyung grew nervous under their gaze, "oh-uh-hi, I'm Taehyung," he quickly bowed to them, stuttering. Meanwhile, Jimin was literally facepalming because of his idiocy.
The boys had chuckled at his nervousness, and the leader of the group had stepped forward. "Nice to meet you, Taehyung, I'm S. Coups."
Tae was practically shaking at that point as the rest of them had introduced themselves. When it got to Joshua, his eyes had widened again, "hey, you're her favorite member!"
The other members had looked to him with confusion. Joshua looked rather surprised himself, as he ended up pointing a finger at his face, as if asking, wait, me? The others had rolled their eyes at him, and Jeonghan had lightly slapped his shoulder, whispering, "yes you, pabo."
"really?" he'd hummed, "Hoseok didn't tell me that."
