Joshua didn't seem to understand the issue as he'd nodded slowly, "Yeah, he asked us to perform for his friend's birthday, Katarina right? He didn't really mention much more than that we're her favorite group and her favorite songs by us."
To say the two boys were dumbfounded was an understatement.
"O-oh," Taehyung had cleared his throat, realizing he couldn't exactly explain the issue at hand as it would be like saying hey by the way, we're breaking the contract, and he didn't know them well enough to know if they were trustworthy with anything like that, "well yeah, she loves you guys tons, especially you, Joshua, seriously she never shuts up about you."
The boy seemed rather flattered by Taehyung's information, "Really? No wonder why Hoseok said to perform Falling For U."
The two boys had soon awkwardly excused themselves from the group of idols, remembering the task at hand. They were also too dumbfounded and mindblown to speak anymore to them, already having a feeling that the fact Hoseok had got them there and not Yoongi would most likely cause a whole shit storm that they definitely didn't want to be a part of.
Making their way towards the side of the room where Hailey was still hiding, meanwhile the poor pink haired girl felt her nerves rising. I'm really doing this? How the hell am I going to do this? were some of the many questions dancing around her head frantically. She watched as the two boys she had missed so desperately were walking right towards her, but they didn't see her yet.
If she was fast enough, she could most likely make a break for the door and actually make it out without them seeing her. All they would hear is the door closing, meaning they would probably check who it was, assuming it would be her. This would mean she'd have to also break for it once she was outside -- which would be a lot of running she didn't know if she could pull off.
The doctor said you weren't supposed to be doing those sorts of things while pregnant. Like planning to meet up with both of the possible fathers before changing your mind last second and running for your life like a lunatic, she thought sarcastically, shaking her head in disbelief at the fact she was really in this situation right now.
It's either I talk to them or run for it, she told herself. She knew she planned to do the first one all this time, but now that it was actually time she was terrified. How were they going to react? She didn't want to hurt Taehyung. She didn't want them to hate her.
Thinking for another moment as she remained hidden in the dark corner, she watched as they searched around the area, calling her name in confusion.
No way, she was shaking from fear and stress, I can't do this.
Turning away from them and towards the door, it was only feet away. All she had to do was run.
Telling herself she had this, she stepped out one foot in front of the other, forcing her body to run despite her enormous belly. Hang in there, she told herself as if she was talking to the life growing inside of her, continuing to run, hoping to make it to the door in time.
When everything seemed to fall, fall like dead leaves.
The feeling of her insides practically crumbling was felt. Her entire body seemed to be giving up, choking almost. She stopped moving to clutch her stomach, bending down and cursing to herself, to think she was almost there, but the running she'd performed had been way too much.
She suddenly felt pants getting wet, her eyes bulged as she tried to process just what was happening. her eyes shot down to her crotch, to see blood.
Meanwhile, Taehyung and Jimin had been searching for her in confusion. Taehyung was confused to say the least, why had she asked them to meet her here and then not show up? Was it some sort of joke? He thought she in Busan, at least that was what kat said.
None of him could seem to understand. Just as he was about to give up, he heard a moan of agony coming from near the back entrance. Jimin had heard it clearly too, and the both of them turned in pure worry at who it was.
They definitely hadn't expected it to be her.
The both of them couldn't process what was happening. The sight of Hailey bending over, clutching her stomach, that was rather large. Everyone get's a food belly, but that definitely wasn't one.
Taehyung couldn't think straight, he had no idea what was happening. All he knew to do was run towards her, realizing that there was something wrong with her and that she needed help.
He especially knew this for sure when he saw the blood pouring from between her legs. The both of their hearts were beating fast, and neither of them knew what to think. She's pregnant, but since when?!
Jimin couldn't believe his eyes. But it all made sense now.
That's why she disappeared for so long.
That's why she wouldn't reply to anyone.
He knew well of the situation from the pieces he had put together in his head. But the real question Jimin wondered was who the hell is the father?
"Hails, oh my god," Taehyung was panicking as he held her, meanwhile she was trembling in his arms, accepting his embrace, "what's going on? what's happening?" Taehyung was too much of a child to understand the situation fully. He'd never seen a woman's water break before, and he couldn't seem to get the fact the girl he loved was having a baby.
"Fuck!" she'd screamed, and no doubt the Seventeen boys were confused as to what was going on, too. They were most likely too afraid to interrupt the situation.
"There's no way this is happening," Jimin had mumbled to himself in disbelief, pulling at his hair in complete stress, "we have to get her to a hospital."
"But... I don't understand what's going on," Taehyung was frowning in concern as he continued to hug the crying girl, who was in excruciating amounts of pain
Through out the pain she managed to find the words she needed, and then she didn't care that both of them knew, it was too late and too obvious. So, without a second thought as to what the both of them might be thinking, she yelled, "my water broke."

***

Break up with Yoongi, or the entirety of Bangtan Sonyeondan's career is over.
The words repeated in her head over and over, it was hypnotizing her at that point. She heard them in that bitch's voice repeatedly, taunting her even in her own brain.
Samantha had left her there after saying that, telling her she would be waiting after giving her her phone number. You have an hour, she'd told her sternly before disappearing into the wind like some sort of ninja. Katarina didn't care to look where she had gone, she didn't care about anything anymore.
Blinded by the tears, her heart ached as she had walked inside the nightclub. through the tears that welled in her green eyes before trickling down her skin, smearing her nicely done makeup and getting mascara everywhere, she walked inside to the sight of Min Yoongi. He had a bandana on like he knew she loved, matched with that stupid jacket he always wore that she loved to steal. He'd walked up to her with a huge smile, walking to embrace her as everyone had jumped out of their hiding spots, yelling, "happy birthday, Katarina!"
It was supposed to be the best moment of her life.
And now it was going to be remembered by her as the worst.
Everyone had screamed her name cheerfully, before the music had been queued and everything had gone insane. Yoongi had pulled away from the embrace after whispering, "happy birthday, jagiya," in her ear. Throughout the entire time, the boy hadn't noticed the tears streaming down his girlfriend's face.
Poor Yoongi had thought everything was perfect finally. His girlfriend had gotten there safely, and there had been no sign of that vile bitch, or so he thought.
Pulling away, he'd looked down at her, his smile immediately vanishing once he saw her teary eyes. "yah," he was instantly concerned, quickly raising his thumbs to wipe them from her face, "jagi, what's wrong?"
But she couldn't find words. She didn't have any words. All Katarina could do was burst into a million sobs at once, stepping forward to hug him as tightly as she possibly could, will all of her might. She wrapped her frail arms around his torso and squeezed him like her life depended on it, and it honestly did.
He didn't hesitate to hug her back, having no idea what was going on but wanting to comfort her in anyway he could. Yoongi rubbed the back of her head, kissing her hair repeatedly as he whispered in her ear for her to calm down.
Forcing her back by putting his hands on her shoulders, he held her up steadily, bending down so she had to meet his pretty brown eyes, his pretty brown eyes I can never admire again, "tell me what's wrong, do you not like the party?"
Trying to breathe from how much she was crying, Katarina hurriedly shook her head. Inhaling air over and over sharply, she tried to catch her breathe but it was pending to be too hard for her. She didn't feel alive anymore, she didn't feel real, nothing around her felt real.
At her sudden irregular breathing, Yoongi had a good feeling to what was happening. She's having an anxiety attack.
"Hey, hey, it's okay," he told her, shushing her calmingly while he dug for his keys in his back pocket, "I'm going to take you home, okay?"
She tried to gather the courage to shake her head, she knew she had to do it. I only have an hour, her mind kept screaming at her.
If only she could've stopped and enjoyed the party he'd worked so hard on for her. If only what he'd intended to happen could've happened. If only she could've seen her favorite group perform like Hoseok had intended, all while she would scream the lyrics and squeal when she saw Joshua. If only she could've danced with her boyfriend to the music, drink with her best friends. If only she could've seen her best friend have her first child.
Yoongi had wrapped his arm protectively around her shoulder, dragging her outside into the night. The air was cold, and he didn't care if anyone saw them leave together. He made sure he would text the others to take care of everything at the party and what had happened. He didn't care much about it anymore, all he cared about was taking care of his girl.
He'd taken off that same jacket to wrap around her shoulders, and she continued to tremble in his arms, still uncontrollably sobbing. He didn't know how to get her to stop as he had no idea what was wrong in the first place. All he knew to do was repeatedly assure her whatever it was would be okay, and that he loved her.
It wasn't long until they'd reached his black camaro. That same camaro they went on their first official date in, that same camaro she'd drove to college with everyday, that one Yoongi had lended to her saying I know it's your favorite car, that's why I bought it.
Escorting her in the car, he had climbed into the drivers seat. Katarina was still shaking, coughing every now in then. She pulled the jacket tighter around her frail body, trying to stop the tears and her aching heart but it was impossible.
As he'd started the car, her eyes dared to look over to the time that read from the stereo.
9:21
She had nine minutes.
Nine minutes to say goodbye to the best relationship she'd ever been in, the one that had meant the world to her. For ever since she'd met Yoongi he caught her eye and she'd fell for him. It was like some sort of fairy tale, all up until that night.
It angered her but broke her at the same time. That bitch, she didn't even know her but for her to do something like this, she had to be fucking insane. It was still so hard for her to believe it was happening, as Yoongi had pulled out of the driveway to the nightclub.
A slow, instrumental song had played softly from the radio, and Katarina continued to silently cry as she tried to grow the courage. I have to do it, I only have seven minutes, she kept telling herself, checking the clock every few seconds out of fear.
Yoongi had been seemingly quiet, not wanting to bother her because he didn't want to make her freak out more. He had just drove in what he thought had been a peaceful silence, not knowing of what was going on inside his girlfriend's head.
If only either of them could've controlled it.
"Yoongi," her voice was hoarse as she finally spoke his name.
The sound of her small, mouse-like voice caused him to look to her while still driving through the dark night in Daejeon.
"What's up, Jagi?" he tried to say casually and not let her know he was shitting himself with worry about her and what had her so upset. He hated seeing her this torn up over whatever it was, maybe it was Jungkook. Had he done something to her? Yoongi swore he would fucking kill him for ruining her night.
"I-," is the only word she could seem to make out. Her heart was broken, but it still wouldn't let her. It wouldn't let her say it, she couldn't do it.
"what is it?" Yoongi had asked, already getting distracted by what it was she had to say. He ended up swerving a bit as he drove, before focusing again on the road and hurriedly getting on the right lane once again.
The music playing from the radio felt like it was taunting her at that point. She swore she could hear Samantha's voice, yelling to her to just do it. Her green eyes dared to look to the time again -- a minute.
She didn't know how close it was until it would hit 9:30. She didn't know why she was so scared to go over the time limit in the first place, it wasn't like Samantha was watching her. But Katarina was too scared, she was too scared of the thought that she would ruin everything for her seven friends.
Telling herself that she had no choice, she'd blurted, "I can't be with you anymore, Yoongi, we have to break up."
Yoongi's heart seemed to shatter in his chest, and everything seemed to happen too fast for anyone to comprehend.
Had he just heard her correctly?
Was he dreaming?
He didn't know. He didn't know anything.
"What?! What are you talking about?!" he'd turned to stare at her with wide eyes, not giving a single shit about where the hell he was driving anymore. He had to understand what the fuck was going on.
"I'm breaking up with you, Min Yoongi."
He couldn't believe what his ears were hearing. After everything? What could've caused her to want to do such a thing? Had Jungkook done something?
Suddenly, as he'd been too awestruck, stuck staring at her meaning he wasn't looking at the road, Yoongi seemed to realize. He seemed to realize just what had happened.
Samantha.
"Wait, it was her wasn't it? Katarina, you don't have to worry about her, I'll take care of it," he continued to steer the wheel even though he wasn't looking at the road, trying to convince her it was okay.
"I'm sorry, Yoongi," she shook her head, tears continuing to flow from her eyes, "I can't take the chance, we can't be together anymore."
It's an unfortunate thing that that was the last thing they'd said to each other. That was the last words Yoongi had heard from his beloved ex girlfriend, as he'd finally gotten paid back for not paying attention to the road like you're always taught in driving school. The sudden impact of a car smashing into the front of Yoongi's jet black camaro caused the both of them to scream, Katarina's high pitched scream echoing through what felt like the entire town. The quick impact would make anyone know for sure, anyone involved was dead.
As it had happened, the front windshield being smashed along with the hood. The two of their bodies being flung forward, the airbags not being much of a help, but more like making it worse. The wind was blowing on that cold night as whoever had been in the other car was most likely gone, too.
How unfortunate, little did they know how familiar of a face the driver of the other car was, as the smoke from the impact had dyed down from the breeze carrying it away. The last thing you'd see was a certain, now crumbled piece of paper flying away with the debris...
